### [1] [AIDA-ReID: Adaptive Intermediate Domain Adaptation for Generalizable and Source-Free Person Re-Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00111)
*Sundas Iqbal,Qing Tian,Danish Ali,Jianping Gou,Weihua Oue*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出自适应中间域适应（AIDA/SF-MIDA）框架，通过动态调控特征混合与正则化强度，实现无需源数据的多源域适应行人重识别，有效解决域偏移问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有中间域方法（如IDM、IDM++）依赖固定的混合策略和联合源-目标域访问，限制了其在多源和无源场景下的适用性。本文旨在克服这些局限，实现更灵活、自适应的域适应。

Method: 提出AIDA框架，将中间域学习视为动态调控过程：利用模型不确定性和训练稳定性反馈信号自适应控制特征混合与正则化强度；设计多源中间域生成器合成多样化中间表示；采用伪镜像正则化策略保持域扰动下的身份一致性。

Result: 在域泛化和无源场景下的广泛实验证明了所提框架的有效性。

Conclusion: AIDA通过自适应调控机制克服了固定混合策略的局限，在无需源数据访问的多源域适应行人重识别任务中取得了优异性能。

Original Abstract: Person re-identification (Re-ID) aims to match images of the same individual across non-overlapping camera views and remains challenging due to domain shifts caused by variations in illumination, background, camera characteristics, and population distributions. Although supervised models perform well under matched training and testing conditions, their performance degrades significantly when deployed in unseen environments. Existing intermediate domain approaches such as IDM and IDM++ alleviate this gap by constructing bridge feature distributions between domains; however, they rely on fixed mixing strategies and joint source-target access, limiting their applicability to multi-source and source-free settings. To address these limitations, this paper proposes Adaptive Intermediate Domain Adaptation (AIDA), also referred to as Source-Free Multi-Source Intermediate Domain Adaptation (SF-MIDA). The proposed framework treats intermediate-domain learning as a dynamically regulated process, where feature mixing and regularization strength are adaptively controlled using feedback signals derived from model uncertainty and training stability. A multi-source intermediate domain generator synthesizes diverse intermediate representations, while a pseudo-mirror regularization strategy preserves identity consistency under domain perturbations. Extensive experiments across domain generalization and source-free settings demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework.

中文摘要翻译: 行人重识别（Re-ID）旨在跨非重叠摄像头视角匹配同一人的图像，但由于光照、背景、摄像头特性和人群分布变化导致的域偏移，该任务依然具有挑战性。尽管监督模型在匹配的训练和测试条件下表现良好，但在部署到未见过的环境时性能显著下降。现有的中间域方法如IDM和IDM++通过构建域间的桥梁特征分布来缓解这一差距，但它们依赖固定的混合策略和联合源-目标域访问，限制了其在多源和无源场景下的适用性。为解决这些局限，本文提出自适应中间域适应（AIDA），也称为无源多源中间域适应（SF-MIDA）。所提出的框架将中间域学习视为动态调控过程，利用从模型不确定性和训练稳定性中导出的反馈信号自适应控制特征混合与正则化强度。多源中间域生成器合成多样化的中间表示，而伪镜像正则化策略在域扰动下保持身份一致性。在域泛化和无源场景下的广泛实验证明了所提框架的有效性。

</details>


### [2] [From Images2Mesh: A 3D Surface Reconstruction Pipeline for Non-Cooperative Space Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00147)
*Bala Prenith Reddy Gopu,Patrick Quinn,George M. Nehma,Madhur Tiwari,Matt Ueckermann,David Hinckley,Christopher McKenna*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于神经隐式表面重建的管线，用于从单目巡检影像中重建非合作空间目标的三维几何结构。该管线结合了基于分割的背景去除、光度校正和相机位姿估计，并在真实的在轨巡检视频（STS-119任务和国际空间站拍摄的H-IIA火箭上面级）上进行了验证。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的神经隐式表面重建方法大多局限于合成数据或已知相机位姿、可控光照的半实物仿真数据，无法直接应用于真实的在轨单目巡检影像。因此，需要开发一种能够处理真实在轨数据中背景变化、光照变化和未知相机位姿等挑战的重建管线。

Method: 提出了一套完整的管线：首先对单目巡检影像进行基于分割的背景去除，然后进行光度校正以补偿帧间曝光差异，接着估计相机位姿，最后利用神经隐式表面重建方法（如NeRF类方法）重建非合作空间目标的三维几何结构。

Result: 1) 基于分割的背景去除对于成功估计真实在轨影像的相机位姿至关重要，否则背景帧间变化会导致直接处理完全失败。2) 光度校正能够有效补偿帧间曝光变化，但在阴影区域的重建性能受输入影像光照特性的影响。

Conclusion: 该管线能够在真实在轨巡检影像上实现非合作空间目标的神经隐式表面三维重建，并验证了背景分割和光度校正是关键预处理步骤。

Original Abstract: On-orbit inspection imagery is crucial as it enables characterization of non-cooperative resident space objects, providing the geometry and structural condition essential for active debris removal and on-orbit servicing mission planning. However, most existing neural implicit surface reconstruction methods have been confined to synthetic or hardware-in-the-loop data with known camera poses and controlled illumination. In this work, we present a pipeline for neural implicit surface reconstruction of non-cooperative space objects from monocular inspection imagery. We demonstrate it on publicly released ISS inspection footage from the STS-119 mission and publicly released on-orbit inspection footage of an H-IIA rocket upper stage. We find that segmentation-based background removal is essential for successful camera pose estimation from real on-orbit footage, where background variation between frames caused direct processing to fail entirely. We further incorporate photometric correction of per-frame exposure variations and analyze its behavior across datasets, finding that performance in shadowed regions varies with the illumination characteristics of the input footage.

中文摘要翻译: 在轨巡检图像至关重要，因为它能够表征非合作空间目标，提供主动碎片清除和在轨服务任务规划所需的几何形状与结构状态信息。然而，现有的大多数神经隐式表面重建方法仅限于合成数据或已知相机位姿且光照受控的半实物仿真数据。本文提出了一套从单目巡检影像中重建非合作空间目标的神经隐式表面重建管线。我们分别在STS-119任务中公开的国际空间站巡检视频以及一枚H-IIA火箭上面级的公开在轨巡检视频上进行了验证。我们发现，基于分割的背景去除对于从真实在轨影像中成功估计相机位姿至关重要，因为帧间背景变化会导致直接处理完全失败。我们进一步引入了光度校正以补偿帧间曝光变化，并在多个数据集上分析了其行为，发现阴影区域的重建性能随输入影像的光照特性而变化。

</details>


### [3] [VkSplat: High-Performance 3DGS Training in Vulkan Compute](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00219)
*Jingxiang Chen,Mohamed Ibrahim,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VkSplat 是一个完全基于 Vulkan compute 实现的高性能、跨厂商的 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) 训练管线，相比 CUDA+PyTorch 基线实现了 3.3 倍加速和 33% 显存节省，且保持渲染质量与跨厂商兼容性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有 3DGS 训练管线依赖 CUDA+PyTorch，存在性能瓶颈和跨 GPU 厂商兼容性受限的问题，亟需一个高性能且通用的替代方案。

Method: 完全基于 Vulkan compute API 实现 3DGS 训练管线，并引入多种底层计算优化，包括但不限于计算着色器调度、内存管理和并行化策略。

Result: 相比 CUDA+PyTorch 基线，VkSplat 实现 3.3 倍训练速度提升和 33% 显存占用减少，同时保持相同的渲染质量，并在不同 GPU 厂商的硬件上验证了兼容性。

Conclusion: VkSplat 是首个完全基于 Vulkan 且达到当前最优性能的 3DGS 训练管线，证明了 Vulkan compute 在 3DGS 训练中作为 CUDA 高效替代方案的可行性。

Original Abstract: We present VkSplat, a high-performance, cross-vendor 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) training pipeline implemented fully in Vulkan compute, addressing performance and compatibility limitation of existing training pipelines. With various optimizations, we achieve $3.3\times$ speed and $33\%$ VRAM reduction over CUDA+PyTorch baseline, maintaining quality, and demonstrating compatibility across GPU vendors. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first fully-Vulkan-based 3DGS training pipeline that achieves state-of-the-art performance. Code: \href{https://github.com/harry7557558/vksplat}{https://github.com/harry7557558/vksplat}

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了 VkSplat，一个完全基于 Vulkan compute 实现的高性能、跨厂商 3D 高斯泼溅（3DGS）训练管线，解决了现有训练管线在性能和兼容性上的局限。通过多种优化，我们在保持渲染质量的同时，相比 CUDA+PyTorch 基线实现了 3.3 倍加速和 33% 的显存降低，并在多个 GPU 厂商的硬件上验证了兼容性。据我们所知，这是首个完全基于 Vulkan 且达到当前最优性能的 3DGS 训练管线。代码开源：\href{https://github.com/harry7557558/vksplat}{https://github.com/harry7557558/vksplat}

</details>


### [4] [SIMON: Saliency-aware Integrative Multi-view Object-centric Neural Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00401)
*YuSheng Lin,Ji-Hwa Tsai,Chun-Shu Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SIMON，一种基于显著性感知的多视图框架，用于零样本EEG到图像检索，通过前景分割和显著性预测选择注视中心并生成注视视图，有效解决了中心偏置问题，在THINGS-EEG数据集上取得最佳性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有EEG-to-image检索方法假设固定的中心注视视角，这与人类内容驱动的注意力机制存在矛盾，导致视觉特征与EEG响应之间存在几何-语义分离（中心偏置问题）。

Method: 提出SIMON框架，包含：(1) 显著性感知采样（SAS），结合前景分割和显著性预测来选择注视中心；(2) 生成注视视图，强调信息丰富的目标区域同时抑制背景杂波；(3) 多视图融合策略。

Result: 在THINGS-EEG数据集上，受试者内设置平均Top-1准确率达69.7%，受试者间设置达19.6%，均优于现有方法。还分析了采样粒度、EEG通道拓扑和视觉/脑编码器骨架的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 显著性感知的多视图融合策略能有效缓解中心偏置问题，提升EEG到图像检索的性能，代码和模型已开源。

Original Abstract: Recent EEG-to-image retrieval methods leverage pretrained vision encoders and foveation-inspired priors, but typically assume a fixed, center-focused view. This center bias conflicts with content-driven human attention, creating a geometric-semantic dissociation between visual features and EEG responses. We propose SIMON, a saliency-aware multi-view framework for zero-shot EEG-to-image retrieval. SIMON combines foreground segmentation and saliency prediction to select fixation centers via Saliency-Aware Sampling (SAS), then generates foveated views that emphasize informative object regions while suppressing background clutter. On THINGS-EEG, SIMON achieves state-of-the-art performance in both intra-subject and inter-subject settings, reaching an average Top-1 accuracy of 69.7% and 19.6%, respectively, consistently outperforming recent competitive baselines. Analyses across sampling granularity, EEG channel topology, and visual/brain encoder backbones further support the robustness of saliency-aware multi-view integration. Our code and models are publicly available at https://github.com/simonlink666/SIMON.

中文摘要翻译: 现有的脑电到图像检索方法利用了预训练的视觉编码器和基于注视的先验知识，但通常假设一个固定的、中心聚焦的视图。这种中心偏置与内容驱动的人类注意力相矛盾，导致视觉特征与脑电响应之间产生几何-语义分离。我们提出了SIMON，一种用于零样本脑电到图像检索的显著性感知多视图框架。SIMON结合了前景分割和显著性预测，通过显著性感知采样（SAS）选择注视中心，然后生成强调信息性目标区域同时抑制背景杂波的注视视图。在THINGS-EEG数据集上，SIMON在受试者内和受试者间设置中均达到了最先进的性能，平均Top-1准确率分别达到69.7%和19.6%，持续优于近期具有竞争力的基线方法。对采样粒度、脑电通道拓扑以及视觉/脑编码器骨架的分析进一步支持了显著性感知多视图融合的鲁棒性。我们的代码和模型已在https://github.com/simonlink666/SIMON公开。

</details>


### [5] [Learning from Compressed CT: Feature Attention Style Transfer and Structured Factorized Projections for Resource-Efficient Medical Image Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00448)
*Shadid Yousuf,S. M. Mahbubur Rahman,Mohammed Imamul Hassan Bhuiyan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对胸部CT体积数据计算开销大的问题，提出CT-Lite框架，利用JPEG压缩输入和轻量化蒸馏方法（FAST + SFP），在显著减少参数的同时实现接近无损输入基线的异常检测性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 医学影像AI部署受限于高计算复杂度和体积数据的资源密集型处理；胸部CT虽比投影放射学提供更丰富诊断信息，但处理未压缩体积图像（如NIfTI/DICOM）的计算负担限制了其在AI诊断中的应用；需要低资源部署和高效电子数据传输。

Method: 提出FAST（特征注意力风格迁移）蒸馏框架，将高保真CT表示中的激活模式和结构关系迁移到处理压缩输入的时空视觉编码器上，通过基于Gram矩阵的注意力风格保持与双注意力特征对齐实现鲁棒特征提取；提出SFP（结构化因子投影），利用块张量链分解作为密集投影层的参数高效替代，将投影头参数减少近一半；将上述组件与SigLIP多模态对齐目标结合形成对比学习流程CT-Lite。

Result: 在CT-RATE、NIDCH和Rad-ChestCT三个数据集上，CT-Lite在使用压缩输入且参数显著减少的情况下，AUROC仅比无损输入基线低5-7%。

Conclusion: CT-Lite实现了在资源受限条件下进行基于AI的临床评估的可行方案，压缩输入带来的性能损失可控。

Original Abstract: The deployment of artificial intelligence in medical imaging is hindered by high computational complexity and resource-intensive processing of volumetric data. Although chest computed tomography (CT) volumes offer richer diagnostic information than projection radiography, their use in AI-based diagnosis remains limited due to the computational burden of processing uncompressed volumetric images (typically stored in NIfTI or DICOM format). Addressing the growing need for low-resource deployment and efficient electronic data transfer, we investigate the utilization of JPEG-compressed chest CT volumes for thoracic abnormality detection. We propose Feature Attention Style Transfer (FAST), a novel distillation framework that transfers both activation patterns and structural relationships from high-fidelity CT representations to a spatiotemporal visual encoder operating on compressed inputs. By combining Gram-matrix-based attention style preservation with dual-attention feature alignment, FAST enables robust feature extraction from degraded volumes. Furthermore, we introduce Structured Factorized Projection (SFP), leveraging Block Tensor Train decomposition as a parameter-efficient alternative to dense projection layers, reducing projection-head parameters by almost half. Our contrastive learning pipeline, CT-Lite, integrates these components with a SigLIP-based multimodal alignment objective. Experiments on CT-RATE, NIDCH, and Rad-ChestCT demonstrate that CT-Lite achieves AUROC within 5-7\% of the uncompressed-input baseline across all three datasets, despite operating on compressed inputs with significantly fewer parameters, paving the way for AI-based clinical evaluation under resource constraints.

中文摘要翻译: 人工智能在医学影像中的部署受到高计算复杂度和体积数据处理资源密集型的阻碍。尽管胸部计算机断层扫描（CT）体积图像比投影放射学提供更丰富的诊断信息，但由于处理未压缩体积图像（通常以NIfTI或DICOM格式存储）的计算负担，其在基于AI的诊断中的应用仍然有限。为应对日益增长的低资源部署和高效电子数据传输需求，我们研究了利用JPEG压缩的胸部CT体积进行胸腔异常检测的方法。我们提出了特征注意力风格迁移（FAST），这是一种新颖的蒸馏框架，将高保真CT表示中的激活模式和结构关系迁移到处理压缩输入的时空视觉编码器上。通过结合基于Gram矩阵的注意力风格保持与双注意力特征对齐，FAST能够从退化体积中提取鲁棒特征。此外，我们引入了结构化因子投影（SFP），利用块张量链分解作为密集投影层的参数高效替代方案，将投影头参数减少近一半。我们的对比学习流程CT-Lite将这些组件与基于SigLIP的多模态对齐目标相结合。在CT-RATE、NIDCH和Rad-ChestCT上的实验表明，尽管CT-Lite在压缩输入上运行且参数显著减少，其在所有三个数据集上实现了仅比无损输入基线低5-7%的AUROC，为资源约束条件下基于AI的临床评估铺平了道路。

</details>


### [6] [Adaptive Geodesic Conformal Prediction for Egocentric Camera Pose Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00233)
*Aishani Pathak,Hasti Seifi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文发现标准共形预测在自我中心姿态估计中存在严重的条件覆盖缺口（最难的25%帧仅覆盖~60%），并提出DINOv2-Bridge自适应共形预测方法，通过单源参与者的两阶段难度估计器实现跨参与者迁移，将最困难帧的覆盖从~75%提升至~93%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 增强现实和辅助设备中的自我中心姿态估计不仅需要准确预测，还需要保证的不确定区域。标准共形预测虽能提供整体覆盖保证，但在困难帧上存在显著的覆盖缺口，这在实际应用中是不可接受的。

Method: 提出DINOv2-Bridge自适应共形预测方法：一个两阶段难度估计器，在单个源参与者上训练，能够在测试时不需任何图像的情况下跨参与者迁移，从而动态调整阈值以缩小困难帧的条件覆盖缺口。

Result: 1) 标准共形预测在12名参与者、3个预测器和3个时间范围（共108项评估）上，整体90%覆盖下最难25%帧仅覆盖约60%，条件覆盖缺口约30个百分点；2) 提出的测地线SE(3)非一致性分数比欧氏分数能更好识别物理上更难的帧，Q4重叠率仅15-26%，Q4帧的真实相机位移高出2-3倍；3) DINOv2-Bridge将Q4覆盖从~0.75提升至~0.93，同时保持整体覆盖在90%目标。

Conclusion: DINOv2-Bridge自适应共形预测方法能有效消除自我中心姿态估计中的条件覆盖缺口，实现跨参与者的公平覆盖，且无需测试时图像，具有良好的实用价值。

Original Abstract: Egocentric pose estimation for Augmented Reality (AR) and assistive devices requires not just accurate predictions but guaranteed uncertainty regions. Conformal prediction (CP) provides such guarantees without retraining, but we show that standard CP with a single fixed threshold achieves nominal 90% overall coverage while covering only ~60% of the hardest 25% of frames (Q4) -- a ~30 percentage-point conditional coverage gap consistent across 12 participants, 3 predictors, and 3 horizons (108 evaluations) on EPIC-Fields. We further show that a geodesic SE(3) nonconformity score identifies physically harder frames than Euclidean scoring, with only 15-26% Q4 overlap and 2-3x higher ground-truth camera displacement for geodesic Q4 frames. To close the coverage gap, we propose DINOv2-Bridge adaptive CP: a two-stage difficulty estimator trained on a single source participant that transfers cross-participant without any images at test time, improving Q4 coverage from ~0.75 to ~0.93 while maintaining overall coverage at the 90% target.

中文摘要翻译: 增强现实（AR）和辅助设备中的自我中心姿态估计不仅需要准确的预测，还需要保证的不确定区域。共形预测（CP）无需重训练即可提供此类保证，但我们发现，使用单一固定阈值的标准CP在达到整体90%标称覆盖率的同时，对最难的25%帧（Q4）仅覆盖约60%——这一条件覆盖缺口约30个百分点，在EPIC-Fields数据集上的12名参与者、3个预测器和3个时间范围（共108项评估）中一致存在。我们进一步证明，测地线SE(3)非一致性分数比欧氏分数更能识别物理上更难的帧，Q4重叠率仅15-26%，且测地线Q4帧的真实相机位移高出2-3倍。为缩小覆盖缺口，我们提出DINOv2-Bridge自适应共形预测：一个在单个源参与者上训练的两阶段难度估计器，可在测试时不需任何图像地跨参与者迁移，将Q4覆盖从约0.75提升至约0.93，同时保持整体覆盖在90%目标水平。

</details>


### [7] [CMTA: Leveraging Cross-Modal Temporal Artifacts for Generalizable AI-Generated Video Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00630)
*Hang Wang,Chao Shen,Chenhao Lin,Minghui Yang,Lei Zhang,Cong Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出跨模态时间伪影（CMTA）检测框架，利用视觉-文本跨模态空间中语义对齐的时间稳定性差异，实现对AI生成视频的有效检测，在40个子集上达到SOTA性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有AIGV检测方法仅关注单模态或时空伪影，忽略了视觉-文本跨模态空间中丰富的线索，特别是语义对齐的时间稳定性这一关键区分特征。

Method: 提出CMTA框架：使用BLIP生成帧级图像描述，CLIP提取视觉-文本表征；设计粗粒度分支（GRU）建模跨模态对齐的时间波动，细粒度分支（Transformer编码器）捕获帧间细微变化。

Result: 在GenVideo、EvalCrafter、VideoPhy、VidProM四个大规模数据集的40个子集上达到SOTA，且表现出优越的跨生成器泛化能力。

Conclusion: AIGV中存在跨模态时间伪影（CMTA）这一独特指纹，利用该特性设计的CMTA框架能有效检测AI生成视频，且泛化性强。

Original Abstract: The proliferation of advanced AI video synthesis techniques poses an unprecedented challenge to digital video authenticity. Existing AI-generated video (AIGV) detection methods primarily focus on uni-modal or spatiotemporal artifacts, but they overlook the rich cues within the visual-textual cross-modal space, especially the temporal stability of semantic alignment. In this work, we identify a distinctive fingerprint in AIGVs, termed cross-modal temporal artifact (CMTA). Unlike real videos that exhibit natural temporal fluctuations in cross-modal alignment due to semantic variations, AIGVs display unnaturally stable semantic trajectories governed by given input prompts. To bridge this gap, we propose the CMTA framework, a cross-modal detection approach that captures these unique temporal artifacts through joint cross-modal embedding and multi-grained temporal modeling. Specifically, CMTA leverages BLIP to generate frame-level image captions and utilizes CLIP to extract corresponding visual-textual representations. A coarse-grained temporal modeling branch is then designed to characterize temporal fluctuations in cross-modal alignment with a GRU. In parallel, a fine-grained branch is constructed to capture intricate inter-frame variations from integrated visual-textual features with a Transformer encoder. Extensive experiments on 40 subsets across four large-scale datasets, including GenVideo, EvalCrafter, VideoPhy, and VidProM, validate that our approach sets a new state-of-the-art while exhibiting superior cross-generator generalization. Code and models of CMTA will be released at https://github.com/hwang-cs-ime/CMTA

中文摘要翻译: 先进AI视频合成技术的扩散对数字视频真实性构成了前所未有的挑战。现有的AI生成视频（AIGV）检测方法主要关注单模态或时空伪影，但它们忽略了视觉-文本跨模态空间中的丰富线索，尤其是语义对齐的时间稳定性。在这项工作中，我们识别出AIGV中一种独特的指纹，称为跨模态时间伪影（CMTA）。与真实视频因语义变化而表现出自然的跨模态对齐时间波动不同，AIGV在给定输入提示的引导下呈现出异常稳定的语义轨迹。为弥合这一差距，我们提出CMTA框架，一种通过联合跨模态嵌入和多粒度时间建模来捕获这些独特时间伪影的跨模态检测方法。具体而言，CMTA利用BLIP生成帧级图像描述，并利用CLIP提取相应的视觉-文本表征。随后设计了一个粗粒度时间建模分支，使用GRU表征跨模态对齐的时间波动。同时，构建了一个细粒度分支，使用Transformer编码器从集成的视觉-文本特征中捕获复杂的帧间变化。在包括GenVideo、EvalCrafter、VideoPhy和VidProM四个大规模数据集的40个子集上进行的大量实验验证了我们的方法达到了新的最先进水平，同时表现出优越的跨生成器泛化能力。CMTA的代码和模型将在https://github.com/hwang-cs-ime/CMTA发布。

### [8] [MAEPose: Self-Supervised Spatiotemporal Learning for Human Pose Estimation on mmWave Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00242)
*Xijia Wei,Yuan Fang,Kevin Chetty,Youngjun Cho,Nadia Bianchi-Berthouze*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MAEPose 是一种基于掩码自编码的毫米波雷达人体姿态估计方法，直接在雷达频谱视频上学习时空运动感知的通用表征，无需依赖预提取的中间表示或标注数据，在三个数据集上以留一法交叉验证达到了SOTA性能（MPJPE最高提升22.1%），且在零样本旁观者干扰下误差仅增加6.5%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有毫米波雷达人体姿态估计方法通常依赖预提取的稀疏点云或频谱图像作为中间表示，丢弃了雷达视频流中丰富的时空信息，且信号处理增加了系统复杂度；此外，现有方法主要采用端到端有监督学习，无法利用无标注原始视频流学习通用表征。因此，本文旨在提出一种直接处理毫米波雷达频谱视频、无需预提取中间表示、且能利用无标注数据进行自监督预训练的姿态估计方法。

Method: 提出MAEPose，采用掩码自编码（Masked Autoencoding）框架，直接在毫米波雷达频谱视频上学习时空运动感知的通用表征；设计热力图解码器（heatmap decoder）用于多帧姿态估计预测；采用自监督预训练方式，利用无标注原始雷达视频流学习通用表征。

Result: 在三个数据集上基于留一法交叉验证（leave-one-person-out）进行严格统计检验，MAEPose在MPJPE指标上以p<0.05的显著性水平一致优于现有SOTA方法，最高提升22.1%；在零样本旁观者干扰下误差仅增加6.5%，保持鲁棒精度。消融实验验证了预训练和热力图解码器的显著贡献；模态分析表明，使用Range-Doppler视频作为输入比Range-Azimuth或其融合方式获得更好的姿态估计性能且计算成本更低。

Conclusion: MAEPose通过掩码自编码在毫米波雷达频谱视频上直接进行自监督预训练，有效学习时空运动感知的通用表征，避免了复杂信号预处理，显著提升了人体姿态估计的准确性和鲁棒性，同时具备隐私保护优势。

Original Abstract: Millimetre-wave (mmWave) radar offers a more privacy-preserving alternative to RGB-based human pose estimation. However, existing methods typically rely on pre-extracted intermediate representations such as sparse point clouds or spectrogram images, where the rich spatiotemporal information naturally present in radar video streams is discarded for model learning, while such signal processing adds system complexity. In addition, existing solutions are mainly conducted in an end-to-end supervised manner without leveraging unlabelled raw video streams to learn generalized representations. In this study, we present MAEPose, a masked autoencoding-based human pose estimation approach that operates directly on mmWave spectrogram videos. MAEPose learns spatiotemporal motion-aware generalized representations from unlabelled radar video, and leverages its heatmap decoder for multi-frame pose estimation predictions. We evaluate it across three datasets based on leave-one-person-out cross-validation with rigorous statistical testing. MAEPose consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by up to 22.1% in MPJPE p<0.05, and maintains robust accuracy under zero-shot bystander interference with only a 6.5% error increase. Ablation studies confirm that both the pre-training and the heatmap decoder contribute substantially, while modality analysis indicates that leveraging Range-Doppler video as input achieves better pose estimation performance than Range-Azimuth or their fusion, with lower computational cost.

中文摘要翻译: 毫米波雷达相较于基于RGB的人体姿态估计提供了一种更具隐私保护性的替代方案。然而，现有方法通常依赖预提取的中间表示（如稀疏点云或频谱图像），这些方法丢弃了雷达视频流中自然存在的丰富时空信息用于模型学习，同时此类信号处理增加了系统复杂度。此外，现有解决方案主要采用端到端有监督方式进行，未能利用无标注的原始视频流学习通用表征。在本研究中，我们提出了MAEPose，一种基于掩码自编码的人体姿态估计方法，直接在毫米波雷达频谱视频上运行。MAEPose从无标注的雷达视频中学习时空运动感知的通用表征，并利用其热力图解码器进行多帧姿态估计预测。我们基于留一法交叉验证在三个数据集上进行评估，并进行了严格的统计检验。MAEPose在MPJPE指标上以p<0.05的显著性水平一致优于现有最优基线方法，最高提升22.1%；在零样本旁观者干扰下保持鲁棒精度，误差仅增加6.5%。消融研究证实，预训练和热力图解码器均贡献显著；模态分析表明，使用Range-Doppler视频作为输入比Range-Azimuth或其融合方式获得了更好的姿态估计性能，且计算成本更低。

### [9] [Remote SAMsing: From Segment Anything to Segment Everything](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00256)
*Osmar Luiz Ferreira de Carvalho,Osmar Abílio de Carvalho Júnior,Anesmar Olino de Albuquerque,Daniel Guerreiro e Silva*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Remote SAMsing流程，在不修改SAM2或需要训练数据的情况下，通过多遍涂抹算法和上下文填充+最佳匹配合并机制，解决了SAM2在遥感大图上的质量-覆盖权衡和跨瓦片碎片化问题，将覆盖率从30-68%提升至91-98%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: SAM2在自然图像上表现优异，但直接应用于大尺度遥感影像存在两个问题：(1) 掩码生成器存在固有的质量-覆盖权衡，严格阈值导致大量未分割区域，宽松阈值则牺牲掩码质量；(2) 大图必须分块处理，导致物体在瓦片边界处被碎片化。现有方法需要修改模型或额外训练数据，缺乏轻量级解决方案。

Method: 提出Remote SAMsing流程，包含两大核心模块：(1) 多遍涂抹算法：在每块瓦片上重复运行SAM2，每次将已接受的掩码涂黑以简化场景，仅在覆盖率增益停滞时才放宽质量阈值，确保最精确的掩码优先被捕获；(2) 空间一致性处理：采用上下文填充(contextual padding)和无参数最佳匹配合并策略，重构跨瓦片边界的碎片化物体。

Result: 在7个场景(5cm至4.78m GSD)上评估，覆盖率从单遍SAM2的30-68%提升至91-98%。消融实验量化了各组件贡献。逐类评估显示SAM2对离散遥感物体迁移良好(建筑物95%，车辆82-93% Det@0.5)，分割边界精度比SLIC和Felzenszwalb基线高3-8倍。瓦片大小可作为隐式尺度参数，从1000降至250时Det@0.5从56%升至85%，超越SAM2内置多尺度机制。流程可泛化至MNF假彩色影像(99.5% ASA)，可扩展至生产级图像：19.4亿像素Potsdam马赛克达到97%覆盖率且无质量下降。

Conclusion: Remote SAMsing流程无需修改SAM2或训练数据，有效解决了SAM2在遥感大图上的质量-覆盖权衡和跨瓦片碎片化问题，显著提升覆盖率且保持分割质量，具备良好的泛化性和可扩展性，适合生产级遥感图像分割任务。

Original Abstract: SAM2 produces high-quality zero-shot segmentation on natural images, but applying it to large remote sensing scenes exposes two problems: (1) its mask generator faces an inherent quality-coverage trade-off: strict thresholds yield precise masks but leave most of the image unsegmented, while relaxed thresholds increase coverage at the cost of mask quality; and (2) large images must be tiled, fragmenting objects across tile boundaries. We propose Remote SAMsing, an open-source pipeline that solves both problems without modifying SAM2 or requiring training data. For coverage, a multi-pass algorithm runs SAM2 repeatedly on each tile, painting accepted masks black between passes to simplify the scene for the next iteration, and relaxing quality thresholds only when coverage gains stagnate, ensuring that the most precise masks are always captured first. For spatial consistency, contextual padding and a parameter-free best-match merge reconstruct objects fragmented across tile boundaries. Evaluated on seven scenes (5~cm to 4.78~m GSD), the pipeline raises coverage from 30--68\% (single-pass SAM2) to 91--98\%. Ablation experiments quantify the contribution of each component to coverage and detection quality. Per-class evaluation shows that SAM2 transfers well to discrete RS objects (buildings 95\%, cars 82--93\% Det@0.5) with segment boundaries 3--8$\times$ more precise than SLIC and Felzenszwalb baselines. Tile size functions as an implicit scale parameter: reducing it from $1{,}000$ to 250 raises Det@0.5 from 56\% to 85\%, outperforming SAM2's built-in multi-scale mechanism. The pipeline generalizes to MNF false-color imagery without retraining (99.5\% ASA) and scales to production-sized images: a 1.94 billion pixel Potsdam mosaic achieved 97\% coverage without quality degradation.

中文摘要翻译: SAM2在自然图像上能够产生高质量的零样本分割，但将其应用于大尺度遥感场景时暴露了两个问题：(1) 其掩码生成器面临固有的质量-覆盖权衡：严格阈值产生精确掩码但导致图像大部分未被分割，而宽松阈值虽增加了覆盖却牺牲了掩码质量；(2) 大图像必须分块处理，导致物体在瓦片边界处被碎片化。我们提出Remote SAMsing，一个开源流程，它在不修改SAM2或需要训练数据的情况下解决了这两个问题。针对覆盖率问题，多遍算法在每块瓦片上重复运行SAM2，在每次迭代间将已接受的掩码涂黑以简化场景，仅在覆盖率增益停滞时放宽质量阈值，确保最精确的掩码始终被优先捕获。针对空间一致性，上下文填充和无参数最佳匹配合并重构了跨瓦片边界的碎片化物体。在七个场景（5cm至4.78m GSD）上的评估表明，该流程将覆盖率从30-68%（单遍SAM2）提升至91-98%。消融实验量化了每个组件对覆盖率和检测质量的贡献。逐类评估显示，SAM2能很好地迁移到离散遥感物体（建筑物95%，车辆82-93% Det@0.5），其分割边界精度比SLIC和Felzenszwalb基线高3-8倍。瓦片大小可作为隐式尺度参数：将其从1,000降至250时，Det@0.5从56%提升至85%，超越了SAM2内置的多尺度机制。该流程无需重新训练即可泛化至MNF假彩色影像（99.5% ASA），并能扩展至生产级图像：一个19.4亿像素的Potsdam马赛克实现了97%的覆盖率且无质量退化。

### [10] [When Do Diffusion Models learn to Generate Multiple Objects?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00273)
*Yujin Jeong,Arnas Uselis,Iro Laina,Seong Joon Oh,Anna Rohrbach*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文通过引入可控数据集生成框架MOSAIC，系统研究了文本到图像扩散模型在多目标生成中失败的根本原因，发现场景复杂度而非概念不平衡是主要影响因素，计数在低数据场景下尤其难以学习，且组合泛化能力随概念组合缺失增多而崩溃。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 尽管文本到图像扩散模型在视觉保真度上表现出色，但在多目标生成任务中仍然不可靠。现有大量实证证据表明存在这些失败，但其根本原因尚不明确。本文旨在探究这一局限性在多大程度上源于数据本身。

Method: 提出MOSAIC（Multi-Object Spatial relations, Attribution, Counting）——一个用于数据集生成的可控框架。在该框架下，设计两种实验设置：(1) 概念泛化：每个独立概念在训练中被观察到，但数据分布可能不平衡；(2) 组合泛化：特定的概念组合被系统性地排除。通过在不同数据集规模下训练扩散模型来研究这两种机制。

Result: (1) 场景复杂度对多目标生成性能起主导作用，而非概念不平衡；(2) 计数任务在低数据场景下尤其难以学习；(3) 随着训练中缺失的概念组合数量增加，组合泛化能力会彻底崩溃。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了扩散模型在多目标组合生成中的根本局限性，表明需要更强的归纳偏置和更稳健的数据设计来支撑鲁棒的组合生成能力。

Original Abstract: Text-to-image diffusion models achieve impressive visual fidelity, yet they remain unreliable in multi-object generation. Despite extensive empirical evidence of these failures, the underlying causes remain unclear. We begin by asking how much of this limitation arises from the data itself. To disentangle data effects, we consider two regimes across different dataset sizes: (1) concept generalization, where each individual concept is observed during training under potentially imbalanced data distributions, and (2) compositional generalization, where specific combinations of concepts are systematically held out. To study these regimes, we introduce mosaic (Multi-Object Spatial relations, AttrIbution, Counting), a controlled framework for dataset generation. By training diffusion models on mosaic, we find that scene complexity plays a dominant role rather than concept imbalance, and that counting is uniquely difficult to learn in low-data regimes. Moreover, compositional generalization collapses as more concept combinations are held out during training. These findings highlight fundamental limitations of diffusion models and motivate stronger inductive biases and data design for robust multi-object compositional generation.

中文摘要翻译: 文本到图像扩散模型在视觉保真度上取得了令人瞩目的成就，但在多目标生成中仍然不可靠。尽管存在大量关于这些失败的实证证据，其根本原因仍不清楚。我们首先探究这一局限性在多大程度上源于数据本身。为了解耦数据的影响，我们考虑了不同数据集规模下的两种机制：(1) 概念泛化，其中每个独立概念在训练中被观察到，但数据分布可能不平衡；(2) 组合泛化，其中特定的概念组合被系统性地排除。为了研究这些机制，我们引入了MOSAIC（多目标空间关系、属性归因、计数）——一个用于数据集生成的可控框架。通过在MOSAIC上训练扩散模型，我们发现场景复杂度起着主导作用，而非概念不平衡，并且计数在低数据场景下尤其难以学习。此外，随着训练中更多概念组合被排除，组合泛化能力彻底崩溃。这些发现突显了扩散模型的根本局限性，并促使研究者设计更强的归纳偏置和更优的数据策略，以实现鲁棒的多目标组合生成。

</details>


### [11] [Beyond Visual Fidelity: Benchmarking Super-Resolution Models for Large-Scale Remote Sensing Imagery via Downstream Task Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00310)
*Zhili Li,Kangyang Chai,Zhihao Wang,Xiaowei Jia,Yanhua Li,Gengchen Mai,Sergii Skakun,Dinesh Manocha,Yiqun Xie*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了GeoSR-Bench，首个将超分辨率重建与下游地球观测任务（如土地覆盖分类、基础设施测绘等）直接关联的基准数据集，发现传统SR保真度指标（PSNR/SSIM）与下游任务性能之间缺乏正相关甚至存在负相关，揭示了将下游任务纳入SR模型开发与评估的必要性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有超分辨率（SR）研究通常使用PSNR或SSIM等保真度指标评估模型性能，但这些指标无法反映超分图像在土地覆盖分类、生物量估计、变化检测等下游地球观测任务中的实际效用，存在评估与实用之间的脱节。

Method: 构建GeoSR-Bench基准数据集，包含来自约36,000个空间共位、时间对齐、质量控制的图像对，覆盖从500m到0.6m分辨率的多种土地覆盖类型。在该数据集上，对GAN、Transformer、神经算子、扩散模型等9种SR模型进行感知质量和下游任务性能（土地覆盖分割、基础设施测绘、生物物理变量估计）的全面基准测试，共涉及270种实验设置、2个跨平台SR任务、3个下游任务模型和5个下游任务。

Result: 传统SR指标（PSNR/SSIM）的提升与下游任务性能的提升往往不相关，甚至呈现负相关关系，表明这些保真度指标为选择适用于下游任务的优秀SR模型提供的指导十分有限。

Conclusion: 需要将下游任务整合到SR模型的开发和评估流程中，而非仅依赖保真度指标。

Original Abstract: Super-resolution (SR) techniques have made major advances in reconstructing high-resolution images from low-resolution inputs. The increased resolution provides visual enhancement and utility for monitoring tasks. In particular, SR has been increasingly developed for satellite-based Earth observation, with applications in urban planning, agriculture, ecology, and disaster response. However, existing SR studies and benchmarks typically use fidelity metrics such as PSNR or SSIM, whereas the true utility of super-resolved images lies in supporting downstream tasks such as land cover classification, biomass estimation, and change detection. To bridge this gap, we introduce GeoSR-Bench, a downstream task-integrated SR benchmark dataset to evaluate SR models beyond fidelity metrics. GeoSR-Bench comprises spatially co-located, temporally aligned, and quality-controlled image pairs from about 36,000 locations across diverse land covers, spanning resolutions from 500m to 0.6m. To the best of our knowledge, GeoSR-Bench is the first SR benchmark that directly connects improved image resolution from SR models with downstream Earth monitoring tasks, including land cover segmentation, infrastructure mapping, and biophysical variable estimation. Using GeoSR-Bench, we benchmark GAN, transformer, neural operator, and diffusion-based SR models on perceptual quality and downstream task performance. We conduct experiments with 270 settings, covering 2 cross-platform SR tasks, 9 SR models, 3 downstream task models, and 5 downstream tasks for each SR task. The results show that improvements in traditional SR metrics often do not correlate with gains in task performance, and the correlations can be negative, indicating that these metrics provide limited guidance for selecting superior models for downstream tasks. This reveals the need to integrate downstream tasks into SR model development and evaluation.

中文摘要翻译: 超分辨率（SR）技术在从低分辨率输入重建高分辨率图像方面取得了重大进展。分辨率的提升为监测任务提供了视觉增强和实用价值。特别是在基于卫星的地球观测中，SR技术在城市规划、农业、生态学和灾害响应等应用中得到了越来越多的开发。然而，现有的SR研究和基准测试通常使用PSNR或SSIM等保真度指标，而超分图像的真实效用在于支持土地覆盖分类、生物量估计和变化检测等下游任务。为弥合这一差距，我们引入了GeoSR-Bench，一个集成下游任务的SR基准数据集，用于在保真度指标之外评估SR模型。GeoSR-Bench包含来自约36,000个位置的、空间共位、时间对齐且经过质量控制的图像对，覆盖从500米到0.6米分辨率的多种土地覆盖类型。据我们所知，GeoSR-Bench是首个将SR模型带来的图像分辨率提升与下游地球监测任务（包括土地覆盖分割、基础设施测绘和生物物理变量估计）直接关联的SR基准。利用GeoSR-Bench，我们对基于GAN、Transformer、神经算子和扩散模型的SR模型在感知质量和下游任务性能上进行了基准测试。我们开展了涵盖2个跨平台SR任务、9个SR模型、3个下游任务模型以及每个SR任务对应的5个下游任务的270种设置实验。结果表明，传统SR指标的提高通常与任务性能的提升不相关，甚至可能出现负相关，这表明这些指标为选择适用于下游任务的优秀SR模型提供的指导十分有限。这揭示了将下游任务整合到SR模型开发和评估中的必要性。

### [12] [Online Self-Calibration Against Hallucination in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00323)
*Minghui Chen,Chenxu Yang,Hengjie Zhu,Dayan Wu,Zheng Lin,Qingyi Si*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出OSCAR框架，利用模型自身的生成-判别能力差距，通过在线自我校准和MCTS构建偏好数据，有效缓解LVLM的幻觉问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有偏好对齐方法依赖更强模型（如GPT）的离线蒸馏监督，导致学生模型被迫对齐超出其感知能力的细粒度细节，产生"监督-感知不匹配"问题，模型学会猜测而非真正看见。

Method: 提出在线自我校准框架OSCAR，利用LVLM中存在的"生成-判别差距"（模型在判别性验证上比开放式生成更准确），结合蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）和双粒度奖励机制构建偏好数据，并通过直接偏好优化（DPO）迭代优化模型。

Result: 在幻觉基准测试上达到最先进性能，同时提升通用多模态能力。

Conclusion: OSCAR通过在线自我校准方式有效缓解了监督-感知不匹配问题，在减少幻觉的同时提升了模型的通用多模态能力。

Original Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) often suffer from hallucinations, generating descriptions that include visual details absent from the input image. Recent preference alignment methods typically rely on supervision distilled from stronger models such as GPT. However, this offline paradigm introduces a Supervision-Perception Mismatch: the student model is forced to align with fine-grained details beyond its perceptual capacity, learning to guess rather than to see. To obtain reliable self-supervision for online learning, we identify a Generative-Discriminative Gap within LVLMs, where models exhibit higher accuracy on discriminative verification than open-ended generation. Leveraging this capability, we propose \textbf{O}nline \textbf{S}elf-\textbf{CA}lib\textbf{R}ation (OSCAR), a framework that integrates Monte Carlo Tree Search with a Dual-Granularity Reward Mechanism to construct preference data and iteratively refines the model via Direct Preference Optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that OSCAR achieves state-of-the-art performance on hallucination benchmarks while improving general multimodal capabilities.

中文摘要翻译: 大型视觉-语言模型（LVLMs）经常出现幻觉问题，生成包含输入图像中不存在视觉细节的描述。现有的偏好对齐方法通常依赖从更强模型（如GPT）中蒸馏得到的监督信号。然而，这种离线范式引入了"监督-感知不匹配"问题：学生模型被迫对齐超出其感知能力的细粒度细节，从而学会猜测而非真正看见。为了在在线学习中获取可靠的自我监督信号，我们发现了LVLM内部存在的"生成-判别差距"——模型在判别性验证任务上的准确率显著高于开放式生成任务。利用这一能力，我们提出了\textbf{在}线\textbf{自}我\textbf{校}准框架（OSCAR），该框架将蒙特卡洛树搜索与双粒度奖励机制相结合来构建偏好数据，并通过直接偏好优化迭代地精炼模型。大量实验表明，OSCAR在幻觉基准测试上达到了最先进性能，同时提升了通用多模态能力。

### [13] [Pose-Aware Diffusion for 3D Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00345)
*Zihan Zhou,Luxi Chen,Jingzhi Zhou,Yuhao Wan,Min Zhao,Baoyu Fan,Chongxuan Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PAD，一种端到端扩散框架，通过在观测空间中直接合成3D几何体，利用反投影单目深度作为3D几何锚点，实现姿态对齐的3D物体生成，解决了规范-旋转范式中的空间错位和变换模糊问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 解耦的规范-旋转范式存在空间错位和变换模糊性，难以生成姿态对齐的3D物体。

Method: 提出PAD（Pose-Aware Diffusion）框架，将单目深度反投影为部分点云并显式注入作为3D几何锚点，在观测空间中端到端合成3D几何体，摒弃规范假设以实施严格的空间监督。

Result: 在几何对齐和图像到3D对应方面优于最先进方法，并能自然扩展到组合式3D场景重建，在独立生成物体后通过简单联合保持精确空间布局。

Conclusion: PAD通过原生姿态感知生成有效解决姿态模糊性，生成高保真姿态对齐资产，且具备良好的场景级扩展能力。

Original Abstract: Generating pose-aligned 3D objects is challenging due to the spatial mismatches and transformation ambiguities inherent in decoupled canonical-then-rotate paradigms. To this end, we introduce Pose-Aware Diffusion (PAD), a novel end-to-end diffusion framework that synthesizes 3D geometry directly within the observation space. By unprojecting monocular depth into a partial point cloud and explicitly injecting it as a 3D geometric anchor, PAD abandons canonical assumptions to enforce rigorous spatial supervision. This native generation intrinsically resolves pose ambiguity, producing high-fidelity pose-aligned assets. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PAD achieves superior geometric alignment and image-to-3D correspondence compared to state-of-the-art methods. Additionally, PAD naturally extends to compositional 3D scene reconstruction via a simple union of independently generated objects, highlighting its robust ability to preserve precise spatial layouts.

中文摘要翻译: 生成姿态对齐的3D物体具有挑战性，原因在于解耦的规范-旋转范式固有的空间错位和变换模糊性。为此，我们提出了PAD（Pose-Aware Diffusion），一种新颖的端到端扩散框架，直接在观测空间中合成3D几何体。通过将单目深度反投影为部分点云并显式注入作为3D几何锚点，PAD摒弃了规范假设，以实施严格的空间监督。这种原生生成方式从本质上解决了姿态模糊性，生成了高保真的姿态对齐资产。大量实验表明，与最先进方法相比，PAD实现了更优的几何对齐和图像到3D对应。此外，PAD通过独立生成物体的简单联合操作，自然扩展到组合式3D场景重建，凸显了其在保持精确空间布局方面的强大能力。

### [14] [CURE-OOD: Benchmarking Out-of-Distribution Detection for Survival Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00350)
*Wenjie Zhao,Jia Li,Mingrui Liu,Jing Wang,Yunhui Guo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建CURE-OOD基准，定义基于扫描仪参数的训练集、分布内（ID）和分布外（OOD）测试集划分，覆盖四个生存预测任务；引入HazardDev作为面向生存感知的OOD检测简单基线。

Conclusion: CURE-OOD能够系统分析分布偏移对下游生存性能及OOD可检测性的影响，为生存预测中的OOD检测研究提供了标准化评估平台。

Original Abstract: ``How long can I live and remain free of cancer?'' is often the first question a patient asks after receiving a cancer diagnosis and treatment. Recent survival prediction frameworks have shown strong performance using computed tomography (CT) images. However, variations in imaging acquisition introduce out-of-distribution (OOD) samples caused by covariate shifts that undermine model reliability. Despite this challenge, to our knowledge, no existing benchmark systematically studies OOD detection in cancer survival prediction. To address this gap, we introduce the Cancer sURvival bEnchmark for OOD Detection (CURE-OOD), the first benchmark for systematically evaluating OOD detection in survival prediction under controlled acquisition-induced distribution shifts. CURE-OOD defines scanner-parameter-based training, in-distribution (ID), and OOD test splits across four survival prediction tasks. Our experiments show that covariate shifts notably reduce survival prediction performance. It also shows that mainstream classification-oriented OOD detectors can fail in survival prediction. Finally, we include HazardDev as a simple survival-aware reference baseline for OOD detection. CURE-OOD enables systematic analysis of how distribution shifts affect both downstream survival performance and OOD detectability.

中文摘要翻译: “我还能活多久？癌症会不会复发？”这通常是患者在接受癌症诊断和治疗后首先提出的问题。准确的生存预测有助于减轻心理痛苦，并支持风险分层和个体化治疗方案制定。近年来的生存预测框架利用计算机断层扫描（CT）图像展现了强劲性能。然而，成像采集的差异会引入由协变量偏移导致的分布外（OOD）样本，从而损害模型的可靠性。尽管面临这一挑战，据我们所知，目前尚无现有基准系统性地研究癌症生存预测中的OOD检测问题。为填补这一空白，我们提出了CURE-OOD（Cancer sURvival bEnchmark for OOD Detection），这是首个在受控的采集诱导分布偏移下系统性评估生存预测中OOD检测能力的基准。CURE-OOD定义了基于扫描仪参数的训练集、分布内（ID）和分布外（OOD）测试集划分，覆盖四个生存预测任务。实验表明，协变量偏移显著降低了生存预测性能。研究还发现，主流的面向分类的OOD检测器可能在生存预测中失效。最后，我们引入了HazardDev，作为一种简单的面向生存感知的OOD检测参考基线。CURE-OOD能够系统分析分布偏移如何影响下游生存性能及OOD可检测性。

### [15] [RTPrune: Reading-Twice Inspired Token Pruning for Efficient DeepSeek-OCR Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00392)
*Ben Wan,Yan Feng,Zihan Tang,Weizhe Huang,Yuting Zeng,Jia Wang,Tongxuan Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RTPrune提出了一种针对DeepSeek-OCR的两阶段令牌剪枝方法，通过优先保留高范数视觉令牌并在第二阶段基于最优传输理论合并剩余令牌，结合动态剪枝比率，在OmniDocBench上实现了99.47%的准确率和1.23倍的预填充加速。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: DeepSeek-OCR虽然通过视觉-文本压缩降低了长文本处理成本，但视觉令牌仍存在冗余的文本和结构信息；现有针对常规视觉语言模型的令牌剪枝方法由于压缩机制不当，无法保持文本保真度。

Method: 提出RTPrune两阶段令牌剪枝方法：第一阶段优先保留捕获关键文本和结构信息的高范数视觉令牌；第二阶段基于最优传输理论对剩余令牌进行配对合并以实现高效特征聚合；并引入适应令牌相似度和文本密度的动态剪枝比率。

Result: 在DeepSeek-OCR-Large上，仅保留84.25%令牌的情况下，在OmniDocBench上达到99.47%的准确率和1.23倍的预填充加速，实现了最先进的性能。

Conclusion: RTPrune通过洞察DeepSeek-OCR的两阶段解码轨迹，设计了一种专门的令牌剪枝方法，有效平衡了OCR任务的效率与准确性。

Original Abstract: DeepSeek-OCR leverages visual-text compression to reduce long-text processing costs and accelerate inference, yet visual tokens remain prone to redundant textual and structural information. Moreover, current token pruning methods for conventional vision-language models (VLMs) fail to preserve textual fidelity due to improper compression mechanisms. By analyzing the decoding process of DeepSeek-OCR, we find that a distinct two-stage reading trajectory: the model initially prioritizes the majority of high-norm tokens, then subsequently redistributes its attention to the remaining ones. Motivated by this insight, we propose RTPrune, a two-stage token pruning method tailored for DeepSeek-OCR. In the first stage, we prioritize high-norm visual tokens that capture salient textual and structural information. In the second stage, the remaining tokens are paired and merged based on optimal transport theory to achieve efficient feature aggregation. We further introduce a dynamic pruning ratio that adapts to token similarity and textual density for OCR tasks, enabling a better efficiency-accuracy trade-off. Extensive experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, as evidenced by 99.47% accuracy and 1.23$\times$ faster prefill on OmniDocBench, achieved with 84.25% token retention when applied to DeepSeek-OCR-Large.

中文摘要翻译: DeepSeek-OCR利用视觉-文本压缩来降低长文本处理成本并加速推理，然而视觉令牌仍容易包含冗余的文本和结构信息。此外，现有的针对常规视觉语言模型（VLM）的令牌剪枝方法因压缩机制不当而无法保持文本保真度。通过分析DeepSeek-OCR的解码过程，我们发现了一个独特的两阶段读取轨迹：模型首先优先处理大部分高范数令牌，随后将其注意力重新分配到剩余令牌上。受此启发，我们提出了RTPrune，一种专为DeepSeek-OCR设计的两阶段令牌剪枝方法。在第一阶段，我们优先保留捕获显著文本和结构信息的高范数视觉令牌。在第二阶段，基于最优传输理论对剩余令牌进行配对合并，以实现高效的特征聚合。我们进一步引入动态剪枝比率，使其适应OCR任务中的令牌相似度和文本密度，从而实现更好的效率-准确性权衡。大量实验证明了最先进的性能，在OmniDocBench上，当应用于DeepSeek-OCR-Large时，以84.25%的令牌保留率实现了99.47%的准确率和1.23倍的预填充加速。

</details>


### [16] [LIMSSR: LLM-Driven Sequence-to-Score Reasoning under Training-Time Incomplete Multimodal Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00434)
*Huangbiao Xu,Huanqi Wu,Xiao Ke,Yuxin Peng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出LIMSSR框架，将训练阶段模态缺失的多模态学习问题重新定义为条件序列推理任务，利用大语言模型的语义推理能力进行模态插补与融合，无需完整模态数据即可在动作质量评估任务上显著超越现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有不完整多模态学习方法普遍假设训练时所有模态完整可用，这在实际场景中不切实际。本文旨在解决训练阶段也存在模态缺失的更具挑战性的设定，摆脱对"上帝视角"完整数据的依赖。

Method: 将不完整多模态学习重新定义为条件序列推理任务；利用大语言模型的语义推理能力，通过提示引导的上下文感知模态插补和多维表示融合来推断潜在语义；引入掩码感知的双路径聚合机制动态校准幻觉，降低推理不确定性。

Result: 在三个动作质量评估数据集上的大量实验表明，LIMSSR在不依赖完整训练数据的情况下显著优于当前最先进基线方法。

Conclusion: LIMSSR为数据高效的多模态学习建立了新范式，证明了在训练阶段存在模态缺失的条件下，通过大语言模型驱动的序列推理能够有效完成多模态学习任务。

Original Abstract: Real-world multimodal learning is often hindered by missing modalities. While Incomplete Multimodal Learning (IML) has gained traction, existing methods typically rely on the unrealistic assumption of full-modal availability during training to provide reconstruction supervision or cross-modal priors. This paper tackles the more challenging setting of IML under training-time incomplete observations, which precludes reliance on a ``God's eye view'' of complete data. We propose LIMSSR (LLM-Driven Incomplete Multimodal Sequence-to-Score Reasoning), a framework that reformulates this challenge as a conditional sequence reasoning task. LIMSSR leverages the semantic reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models via Prompt-Guided Context-Aware Modality Imputation and Multidimensional Representation Fusion to infer latent semantics from available contexts without direct reconstruction. To mitigate hallucinations, we introduce a Mask-Aware Dual-Path Aggregation to dynamically calibrate inference uncertainty. Extensive experiments on three Action Quality Assessment datasets demonstrate that LIMSSR significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines without relying on complete training data, establishing a new paradigm for data-efficient multimodal learning. Code is available at https://github.com/XuHuangbiao/LIMSSR.

中文摘要翻译: 现实世界中的多模态学习常常受到模态缺失的阻碍。虽然不完整多模态学习（IML）已受到广泛关注，但现有方法通常依赖于训练期间所有模态完全可用这一不切实际的假设，以提供重构监督或跨模态先验。本文针对训练阶段存在不完整观察这一更具挑战性的IML设定展开研究，该设定排除了对完整数据"上帝视角"的依赖。我们提出LIMSSR（大语言模型驱动的不完整多模态序列到分数推理）框架，将该挑战重新定义为条件序列推理任务。LIMSSR利用大语言模型的语义推理能力，通过提示引导的上下文感知模态插补和多维表示融合，从可用上下文中推断潜在语义而无需直接重构。为减轻幻觉，我们引入掩码感知的双路径聚合机制来动态校准推理不确定性。在三个动作质量评估数据集上的大量实验表明，LIMSSR在不依赖完整训练数据的情况下显著优于当前最先进的基线方法，为数据高效的多模态学习建立了新范式。代码开源在 https://github.com/XuHuangbiao/LIMSSR。

### [17] [Scaling Video Understanding via Compact Latent Multi-Agent Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00444)
*Kerui Chen,Jinglu Wang,Jianrong Zhang,Ming Li,Yan Lu,Hehe Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MACF，一种端到端多智能体协作框架，通过解耦感知预算与视频全局复杂度，利用智能体间潜在空间通信，实现长视频的高效、保真理解，显著优于现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有MLLM在长视频任务中受限于有限的感知上下文预算；基于规则的智能体方法存在信息丢失、成本高、依赖文本中间表示等问题，亟需一种端到端、保视觉保真度的可扩展视频理解方案。

Method: MACF将视频分割为片段分配给具有本地预算的智能体，通过智能体原生潜在通信协议实现整体推理：每个智能体将局部观察编码为紧凑、任务充分的潜在token，在共享嵌入空间中由中央协调器进行高效、信息保留的协作。采用课程训练策略，逐步强化语义对齐、证据总结和跨智能体协调。

Conclusion: 提出的潜在协作机制能够有效解耦单智能体感知预算与全局视频复杂度，在保持视觉保真度的同时实现长视频的可扩展理解，为多智能体视频理解提供了新的范式。

Original Abstract: Multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) advance vision language understanding but face inherent limitations in long-video tasks due to bounded perception context budgets. Existing agentic methods mitigate this via rule-based preprocessing, yet often suffer from information loss, high cost, and reliance on textual intermediates. We propose MACF, an end-to-end Multi-Agent Collaboration Framework that decouples per-agent perception budgets from global video complexity, enabling scalable video understanding while preserving visual fidelity. MACF partitions videos into segments for locally budgeted agents and enables holistic reasoning via an agent-native latent communication protocol. Each agent encodes partial observations into compact, task-sufficient tokens in a shared embedding space, allowing efficient and information-preserving collaboration by a central coordinator. We introduce a curriculum training strategy that progressively enforces semantic alignment, evidence summarization, and cross-agent coordination. Extensive experiments on diverse video understanding benchmarks show that MACF consistently outperforms state-of-the-art MLLMs and multi-agent systems under identical budget constraints, demonstrating the effectiveness of our latent collaboration for scalable video understanding.

中文摘要翻译: 多模态大语言模型推动了视觉语言理解的发展，但由于受限的感知上下文预算，在长视频任务中面临固有局限性。现有基于智能体的方法通过规则驱动的预处理缓解这一问题，但常遭受信息损失、高成本以及对文本中间表示的依赖。我们提出MACF，一种端到端的多智能体协作框架，将每个智能体的感知预算与全局视频复杂度解耦，在保持视觉保真度的同时实现可扩展的视频理解。MACF将视频划分为片段分配给具有本地预算的智能体，并通过智能体原生的潜在通信协议实现整体推理。每个智能体将局部观察编码为紧凑的、任务充分的token，映射到共享嵌入空间中，由中央协调器实现高效且保留信息的协作。我们引入一种课程训练策略，逐步强化语义对齐、证据总结和跨智能体协调。在多种视频理解基准上的大量实验表明，在相同预算约束下，MACF一致优于最先进的MLLM和多智能体系统，验证了我们的潜在协作策略在可扩展视频理解中的有效性。

### [18] [From Local to Global to Mechanistic: An iERF-Centered Unified Framework for Interpreting Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00474)
*Yearim Kim,Sangyu Han,Nojun Kwak*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个以实例有效感受野（iERF）为中心的统一可解释性框架，整合了局部、全局和机制性可解释性。该框架包含三个核心组件：共享比率分解（SRD）用于生成高分辨率、忠实于激活的局部显著性图；概念锚定特征解释（CAFE）利用iERF作为语义标签来定位分散的稀疏自编码器潜在变量；层间概念图与层间概念归因（ICAT）用于量化跨层概念间的影响。实验在ResNet50、VGG16和ViT上验证了该框架在保真度和鲁棒性上优于基线方法，并能有效解释正确分类、错误分类及对抗样本中的概念路径。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视觉模型虽精度高，但对其证据来源、编码内容以及内部计算如何组装证据的解释仍较为零散，缺乏一个统一的分析单元来整合局部、全局和机制性可解释性。

Method: 以点状特征向量及其实例有效感受野（iERF）为核心分析单元，提出三个组件：1) 局部层面：共享比率分解（SRD），通过共享比率将每个PFV表示为上游PFV的混合，并传播iERF以构建类别判别性显著性图；2) 全局层面：概念锚定特征解释（CAFE），利用iERF作为语义标签，将抽象潜在向量锚定于可验证的像素级证据；3) 机制层面：层间概念图与层间概念归因（ICAT），量化概念间影响并隔离层对，通过插入/删除协议确定集成梯度为最忠实的实例化方法。

Result: 在ResNet50、VGG16和ViT上的实验表明，所提框架在保真度和鲁棒性上均优于基线方法，能成功解释分散的SAE特征，并在正确分类、错误分类及对抗性样本中揭示主导的概念路径。

Conclusion: 基于iERF的方法提供了一条从像素到概念再到决策的连贯且可验证的映射路径，实现了局部、全局与机制性可解释性的统一。

Original Abstract: Modern vision models achieve remarkable accuracy, but explaining where evidence arises, what the model encodes, and how internal computations assemble that evidence remains fragmented. We introduce an iERF-centric framework that unifies local, global, and mechanistic interpretability around a single analysis unit: the pointwise feature vector (PFV) paired with its instance-specific Effective Receptive Field (iERF). On the local side, Sharing Ratio Decomposition (SRD) expresses each PFV as a mixture of upstream PFVs via sharing ratios and propagates iERFs to construct class-discriminative saliency maps. SRD yields high-resolution, activation-faithful explanations, is robust to targeted manipulation and noise, and remains activation-agnostic across common nonlinearities. For the global view, we introduce Concept-Anchored Feature Explanation (CAFE), which utilizes the iERF as a semantic label, grounding abstract latent vectors in verifiable pixel-level evidence. With CAFE, we address the challenge of non-localized sparse autoencoder latents--especially in Transformers, where early self-attention mixes distant context. To answer how representations are composed through depth, we propose the Interlayer Concept Graph with Interlayer Concept Attribution (ICAT), which quantifies concept-to-concept influence while isolating layer pairs; an interlayer insertion, deletion protocol identifies Integrated Gradients as the most faithful instantiation. Empirically, across ResNet50, VGG16, and ViTs, our framework outperforms baselines in both fidelity and robustness, successfully interprets dispersed SAE features, and exposes dominant concept routes in correct, misclassified, and adversarial cases. Grounded in iERFs, our approach provides a coherent, evidence-backed map from pixels to concepts to decisions.

中文摘要翻译: 现代视觉模型取得了显著的精度，但关于证据从何处产生、模型编码了什么内容以及内部计算如何组装这些证据的解释仍然零散。我们提出一个以iERF为中心的框架，将局部、全局和机制性可解释性统一在一个单一分析单元上：点状特征向量（PFV）与其实例特定有效感受野（iERF）的配对。在局部层面，共享比率分解（SRD）通过共享比率将每个PFV表示为上游PFV的混合，并传播iERF以构建类别判别性显著性图。SRD生成高分辨率、忠实于激活的解释，对定向操控和噪声具有鲁棒性，并且在常见非线性激活函数下保持激活无关性。在全局视角方面，我们引入概念锚定特征解释（CAFE），它将iERF作为语义标签，将抽象潜在向量锚定于可验证的像素级证据。借助CAFE，我们解决了非局部化稀疏自编码器潜在变量的挑战——尤其是在Transformer中，早期自注意力会混合远距离上下文。为了回答表示如何在深度方向上组合而成的问题，我们提出层间概念图与层间概念归因（ICAT），它在隔离层对的同时量化概念间的影响；一种层间插入、删除协议将集成梯度确定为最忠实的实例化方法。实验上，在ResNet50、VGG16和ViT上，我们的框架在保真度和鲁棒性方面均优于基线方法，成功解释了分散的SAE特征，并在正确分类、错误分类及对抗性样本中揭示了主导的概念路径。基于iERF，我们的方法提供了一条从像素到概念再到决策的连贯且可验证的映射路径。

</details>


### [19] [Leveraging Vision-Language Models as Weak Annotators in Active Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00480)
*Phuong Ngoc Nguyen,Kaito Shiku,Ryoma Bise,Seiichi Uchida,Shinnosuke Matsuo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种结合细粒度人工标注与VLM生成的粗粒度弱标签的主动学习框架，通过实例级标签分配和噪声建模，在有限标注预算下提升细粒度识别性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: VLM在细粒度标签上表现差但能提供准确的粗粒度标签，利用这一特性，在主动学习中结合VLM弱标签与人工标注，减少对昂贵人工标注的依赖。

Method: 提出一个主动学习框架：(1) 通过实例级标签分配，将细粒度人工标注与VLM生成的粗粒度弱标签相结合；(2) 使用少量可信完整标签对VLM生成标签中的系统噪声进行建模。

Result: 在CUB200和FGVC-Aircraft数据集上，所提框架在相同标注预算下一致优于现有主动学习方法。

Conclusion: 利用VLM在粗粒度标签上的可靠性，结合细粒度人工标注，可以有效提升主动学习在细粒度识别任务中的性能，降低对昂贵人工标注的依赖。

Original Abstract: Active learning aims to reduce annotation cost by selectively querying informative samples for supervision under a limited labeling budget. In this work, we investigate how vision-language models (VLMs) can be leveraged to further reduce the reliance on costly human annotation within the active learning paradigm. To this end, we find that the reliability of VLMs varies significantly with label granularity in fine-grained recognition tasks: they perform poorly on fine-grained labels but can provide accurate coarse-grained labels. Leveraging this property, we propose an active learning framework that combines fine-grained human annotations with coarse-grained VLM-generated weak labels through instance-wise label assignment. We further model the systematic noise in VLM-generated labels using a small set of trusted full labels. Experiments on CUB200 and FGVC-Aircraft show that the proposed framework consistently outperforms existing active learning methods under the same annotation budget.

中文摘要翻译: 主动学习旨在通过有限标注预算下有选择地查询信息量大的样本进行监督，从而降低标注成本。本文研究如何利用视觉-语言模型（VLM）在主动学习范式中进一步减少对昂贵人工标注的依赖。为此，我们发现VLM在细粒度识别任务中的可靠性随标签粒度变化显著：它们在细粒度标签上表现不佳，但能准确提供粗粒度标签。利用这一特性，我们提出一个主动学习框架，通过实例级标签分配将细粒度人工标注与VLM生成的粗粒度弱标签相结合。我们进一步使用少量可信的完整标签对VLM生成标签中的系统噪声进行建模。在CUB200和FGVC-Aircraft上的实验表明，所提框架在相同标注预算下一致优于现有主动学习方法。

### [20] [High-Speed Vision Improves Zero-Shot Semantic Understanding of Human Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00496)
*Yongpeng Cao,Yuji Yamakawa*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究时间分辨率（帧率）对零样本语义理解高速人体动作的影响。使用剑道作为代表性案例，提出了一种无需训练、结合预训练视频-语言模型和LLM推理的流程，实验表明更高帧率（如120Hz）显著提升零样本语义可分性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 高速、罕见动作难以收集足量标注数据用于监督学习，而现有零样本方法对时间分辨率（尤其对快速细微运动）的影响尚未充分探索。

Method: 提出无需训练流程：预训练视频-语言模型提取语义表征 + 基于大语言模型的成对动作比较推理。在多个帧率（120Hz/60Hz/30Hz）下进行控制实验，并使用最近类原型策略进行定量评估。

Result: 更高时间分辨率（120Hz）显著提升零样本语义可分性；高速视频提供更稳定和可解释的语义表征；在完整和部分观测场景下，基于跟踪的人体关节信息均有效。

Conclusion: 时间分辨率在无需训练的动作识别中至关重要，高速感知能增强对快速动作的语义理解能力。

Original Abstract: Understanding human actions from visual observations is essential for human--robot interaction, particularly when semantic interpretation of unfamiliar or hard-to-annotate actions is required. In scenarios such as rapid and less common activities, collecting sufficient labeled data for supervised learning is challenging, making zero-shot approaches a practical alternative for semantic understanding without task-specific training. While recent advances in large-scale pretrained models enable such zero-shot reasoning, the impact of temporal resolution, especially for rapid and fine-grained motions, remains underexplored.
  In this study, we investigate how temporal resolution affects zero-shot semantic understanding of high-speed human actions. Using kendo as a representative case of rapid and subtle motion patterns, we propose a training-free pipeline that combines a pre-trained video-language model for semantic representation with large language model-based reasoning for pairwise action comparison. Through controlled experiments across multiple frame rates (120 Hz, 60 Hz, and 30 Hz), we show that higher temporal resolution significantly improves semantic separability in zero-shot settings. We further analyze the role of tracking-based human joint information under both full and partial observation scenarios. Quantitative evaluation using a nearest-class prototype strategy demonstrates that high-speed video provides more stable and interpretable semantic representations for fast actions. These findings highlight the importance of temporal resolution in training-free action recognition and suggest that high-speed perception can enhance semantic understanding capabilities.

中文摘要翻译: 从视觉观察中理解人类动作对于人机交互至关重要，尤其是在需要对不熟悉或难以标注的动作进行语义解释时。在快速、不常见活动等场景中，收集足够的标注数据进行监督学习具有挑战性，因此零样本方法成为无需任务特定训练即可实现语义理解的实用替代方案。虽然近期大规模预训练模型的进展支持了这种零样本推理，但时间分辨率的影响——特别是对快速和细微运动——仍未得到充分探索。在本研究中，我们探究了时间分辨率如何影响高速人类动作的零样本语义理解。以剑道作为快速和细微运动模式的代表性案例，我们提出了一种无需训练的流程，该流程结合了预训练视频-语言模型进行语义表征，以及基于大语言模型推理的成对动作比较。通过在多个帧率（120Hz、60Hz和30Hz）下的控制实验，我们证明更高时间分辨率显著提升了零样本场景下的语义可分性。我们进一步分析了在完整和部分观测场景下基于跟踪的人体关节信息的作用。采用最近类原型策略的定量评估表明，高速视频为快速动作提供了更稳定和可解释的语义表征。这些发现凸显了时间分辨率在无需训练的动作识别中的重要性，并表明高速感知能够增强语义理解能力。

### [21] [GOR-IS: 3D Gaussian Object Removal in the Intrinsic Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00498)
*Yonghao Zhao,Yupeng Gao,Jian Yang,Jin Xie,Beibei Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种在内在空间中进行3D高斯物体移除的框架（GOR-IS），通过分解场景为内在成分并显式建模光传输，实现了物理一致且视觉连贯的物体移除，在LPIPS和PSNR上分别提升13%和2dB。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有3D物体移除方法虽然提升了修复一致性，但忽略了全局光照效应，导致结果物理不真实；同时难以处理视点依赖的非朗伯表面，修复结果不可靠。

Method: 将场景分解为内在成分（材质、光照等），显式建模光传输以保持全局光照一致性；引入内在空间修复模块，直接在材质和光照域进行操作，解决非朗伯表面的挑战。

Result: 在合成和真实数据集上，该方法在感知相似度（LPIPS）上提升13%，在峰值信噪比（PSNR）上提升2dB，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: GOR-IS框架通过内在空间分解和显式光传输建模，有效提升了物体移除的物理一致性和视觉连贯性，在非朗伯表面等复杂场景下表现优越。

Original Abstract: Recent advances in Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) and 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have made it standard practice to reconstruct 3D scenes from multi-view images. Removing objects from such 3D representations is a fundamental editing task that requires complete and seamless inpainting of occluded regions, ensuring consistency in geometry and appearance. Although existing methods have made notable progress in improving inpainting consistency, they often neglect global lighting effects, leading to physically implausible results. Moreover, these methods struggle with view-dependent non-Lambertian surfaces, where appearance varies across viewpoints, leading to unreliable inpainting. In this paper, we present 3D Gaussian Object Removal in the Intrinsic Space (GOR-IS), a novel framework for physically consistent and visually coherent 3D object removal. Our approach decomposes the scene into intrinsic components and explicitly models light transport to maintain global lighting effects consistency. Furthermore, we introduce an intrinsic-space inpainting module that operates directly in the material and lighting domains, effectively addressing the challenges posed by non-Lambertian surfaces. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our framework substantially improves the physical consistency and visual coherence of object removal, outperforming existing methods by 13% in perceptual similarity (LPIPS) and 2dB in peak signal-to-noise ratio (PSNR). Code is publicly available at https://applezyh.github.io/GOR-IS-project-page/

中文摘要翻译: 神经辐射场（NeRF）和3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）的最新进展使得从多视图图像重建3D场景成为标准实践。从这类3D表示中移除物体是一项基本的编辑任务，需要对被遮挡区域进行完整且无缝的修复，确保几何和外观的一致性。尽管现有方法在提升修复一致性方面取得了显著进展，但它们往往忽略了全局光照效应，导致结果在物理上不合理。此外，这些方法在处理视点依赖的非朗伯表面时存在困难——这类表面的外观随视角变化，导致修复结果不可靠。在本文中，我们提出了内在空间中的3D高斯物体移除（GOR-IS）框架，这是一种实现物理一致且视觉连贯的3D物体移除的新型框架。我们的方法将场景分解为内在成分，并显式建模光传输以保持全局光照效应的一致性。此外，我们引入了一个内在空间修复模块，该模块直接在材质和光照域中操作，有效应对非朗伯表面带来的挑战。在合成数据集和真实数据集上的大量实验表明，我们的框架显著提升了物体移除的物理一致性和视觉连贯性，在感知相似度（LPIPS）上优于现有方法13%，在峰值信噪比（PSNR）上提升2dB。代码已开源：https://applezyh.github.io/GOR-IS-project-page/

</details>

Method: (1) 将高分辨率人体网格简化为几何基元，大幅降低碰撞检测成本；(2) 识别碰撞区域作为优化方向的引导；(3) PhysiGen作为即插即用模块，可集成到现有交互生成模型中。

Original Abstract: Despite substantial progress in text-driven 3D human motion synthesis, generating realistic multi-person interaction sequences remains challenging. ### [25] [Colorful-Noise: Training-Free Low-Frequency Noise Manipulation for Color-Based Conditional Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00548)
*Nadav Z. Cohen,Ofir Abramovich,Ariel Shamir*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了扩散模型中输入噪声的特性，发现低频成分决定全局结构和颜色，高频成分控制细节。基于此，通过简单的低频噪声操作（利用低频图像先验）即可无需训练地引导图像生成，在保留细节多样性的同时控制整体结构和颜色。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 白高斯噪声虽然能产生多样化的生成结果，但其不可解释的特性限制了用户对生成图像特定视觉属性（如全局结构、颜色）的控制和可预测性。

Method: 分析扩散模型输入噪声的频率特性，发现低频成分主导全局结构与颜色、高频成分控制细节；据此提出一种无需训练、计算开销极小的简单方法：通过低频图像先验对输入噪声的低频部分进行简单操作，从而条件化生成过程，保留高频成分的自由变化以实现多样性。

Result: 白高斯噪声中所有频率统计能量相当，但低频成分主要决定图像全局结构和颜色组成，高频成分控制更精细的细节。基于此发现，对低频噪声的简单操作可以有效引导生成，重构低频视觉线索。

Conclusion: 定义了一种简单、无需训练、额外开销极小的生成控制方法，能够引导图像的整体结构和颜色，同时让高频成分自由涌现为精细细节，保证生成输出的多样性。

Original Abstract: Text-to-image diffusion models generate images by gradually converting white Gaussian noise into a natural image. White Gaussian noise is well suited for producing diverse outputs from a single text prompt due to its absence of structure. However, this very property limits control over, and predictability of, specific visual attributes, as the noise is not human-interpretable. In this work, we investigate the characteristics of the input noise in diffusion models. We show that, although all frequencies in white Gaussian noise have comparable statistical energy, low-frequency components primarily determine the images global structure and color composition, while high-frequency components control finer details. Building on this observation, we demonstrate that simple manipulations of the low-frequency noise using low-frequency image priors can effectively condition the generation process to reconstruct these low-frequency visual cues. This allows us to define a simple, training-free method with minimal overhead that steers overall image structure and color, while letting high-frequency components freely emerge as fine details, enabling variability across generated outputs.

中文摘要翻译: 文本到图像扩散模型通过将白高斯噪声逐渐转换为自然图像来生成图像。白高斯噪声由于其缺乏结构，非常适合从单个文本提示生成多样化的输出。然而，正是这一特性限制了对特定视觉属性的控制和可预测性，因为该噪声是不可人类解释的。在本工作中，我们研究了扩散模型中输入噪声的特性。我们发现，尽管白高斯噪声中所有频率的统计能量相当，但低频成分主要决定图像的全局结构和颜色组成，而高频成分控制更精细的细节。基于这一观察，我们证明利用低频图像先验对低频噪声进行简单操作，可以有效地条件化生成过程，以重构这些低频视觉线索。这使我们能够定义一种简单、无需训练且额外开销极小的方法，用于引导图像的整体结构和颜色，同时让高频成分自由涌现为精细细节，从而实现生成输出的多样性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1）引入单目深度和法线先验来提升几何精度与鲁棒性；2）提出深度引导的高斯原语初始化策略；3）提出基于聚类的退化高斯原语剪枝技术。

### [27] [Jailbreaking Vision-Language Models Through the Visual Modality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00583)
*Aharon Azulay,Jan Dubiński,Zhuoyun Li,Atharv Mittal,Yossi Gandelsman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文揭示了视觉-语言模型（VLM）的视觉模态是绕过安全对齐的未充分探索的攻击面，提出了四种利用视觉组件的越狱攻击，实验表明基于文本的安全训练无法自动泛化到视觉传达的恶意意图，需将视觉作为安全后训练的一类目标。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有VLM的安全对齐主要聚焦于文本模态，视觉模态作为攻击面尚未被充分探索，存在跨模态对齐鸿沟：文本安全训练无法自动泛化到视觉传达的恶意意图。

Method: 提出了四种越狱攻击方法：(1) 将有害指令编码为视觉符号序列并附带解码图例；(2) 用良性替代物替换有害对象（如bomb→banana）并诱导使用替代词执行有害动作；(3) 将图像中的有害文本替换为良性词，但视觉上下文保留原意；(4) 视觉类比谜题，其解答需推断出被禁止的概念。

Result: 在六个前沿VLM上评估，视觉攻击成功绕过了安全对齐。例如，视觉密码对Claude-Haiku-4.5的攻击成功率达40.9%，而等效文本密码仅为10.7%。此外还提供了初步的可解释性和缓解结果。

Conclusion: 鲁棒的VLM对齐需要将视觉模态作为安全后训练的一等公民目标，文本安全训练不足以防御视觉传达的有害意图。

Original Abstract: The visual modality of vision-language models (VLMs) is an underexplored attack surface for bypassing safety alignment. We introduce four jailbreak attacks exploiting the vision component: (1) encoding harmful instructions as visual symbol sequences with a decoding legend, (2) replacing harmful objects with benign substitutes (e.g., bomb -> banana) then prompting for harmful actions using the substitute term, (3) replacing harmful text in images (e.g., on book covers) with benign words while visual context preserves the original meaning, and (4) visual analogy puzzles whose solution requires inferring a prohibited concept. Evaluating across six frontier VLMs, our visual attacks bypass safety alignment and expose a cross-modality alignment gap: text-based safety training does not automatically generalize to harmful intent conveyed visually. For example, our visual cipher achieves 40.9% attack success on Claude-Haiku-4.5 versus 10.7% for an equivalent textual cipher. To further our insight into the attack mechanism, we present preliminary interpretability and mitigation results. These findings highlight that robust VLM alignment requires treating vision as a first-class target for safety post-training.

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言模型（VLM）的视觉模态是绕过安全对齐的一个未充分探索的攻击面。我们引入了四种利用视觉组件的越狱攻击：(1) 将有害指令编码为带有解码图例的视觉符号序列；(2) 用良性替代物替换有害对象（如炸弹→香蕉），然后使用替代词提示模型执行有害动作；(3) 将图像中的有害文本（如书籍封面上的文字）替换为良性词，但视觉上下文保留原始含义；(4) 视觉类比谜题，其解答需要推断出一个被禁止的概念。在六个前沿VLM上进行评估，我们的视觉攻击绕过了安全对齐，并揭示了一个跨模态对齐鸿沟：基于文本的安全训练无法自动泛化到视觉传达的恶意意图。例如，我们的视觉密码对Claude-Haiku-4.5的攻击成功率达到40.9%，而等效文本密码仅为10.7%。为了进一步理解攻击机制，我们提供了初步的可解释性和缓解结果。这些发现表明，鲁棒的VLM对齐需要将视觉模态作为安全后训练的一等公民目标。

</details>


### [28] [Intrinsic Gradient Suppression for Label-Noise Prompt Tuning in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00591)
*Jiayu Li,Jiaxin Qi,Sheng Zhou,Jiaqiang Huang,Xiansheng Hua*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为双Softmax提示调优（DSPT）的无超参数方法，通过内在梯度抑制机制，在含噪标签场景下实现鲁棒的CLIP提示调优，将梯度消失从训练瓶颈转化为噪声过滤屏障。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: CLIP在零样本泛化方面表现优异，但提示调优对标签噪声高度敏感——错误标记样本会产生不成比例的大梯度，可能压倒预训练先验。由于CLIP已提供接近最优的初始化，适应过程应保持保守，尤其在噪声环境下需要抑制极端梯度更新。

Method: 提出双Softmax提示调优（DSPT），通过顺序概率归一化（即两次Softmax操作）诱导出自适应的饱和区域，从而抑制高误差噪声样本的梯度，同时保留信息性更新。该方法无需超参数，是一种即插即用的内在梯度抑制机制。

Result: 理论分析和实验证明DSPT能实现自适应梯度抑制；在多种含噪基准测试中，该简单方法达到了最先进的鲁棒性，优于使用复杂架构和手工设计超参数的方法。

Conclusion: DSPT通过巧妙的双Softmax设计，将传统上被视为训练瓶颈的梯度消失转化为一种有原则的噪声过滤屏障，为含噪标签下的提示调优提供了简洁而有效的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Contrastive vision-language models like CLIP exhibit remarkable zero-shot generalization. However, prompt tuning remains highly sensitive to label noise, as mislabeled samples generate disproportionately large gradients that can overwhelm pre-trained priors. We argue that because CLIP already provides a near-optimal initialization, adaptation should be inherently conservative, particularly against the extreme gradient updates common in noisy settings. To this end, we propose Double-Softmax Prompt Tuning (DSPT), a hyperparameter-free method for intrinsic gradient suppression. By applying a sequential probabilistic normalization, DSPT induces a self-adaptive saturation zone that suppresses gradients from high-error noisy samples while maintaining informative updates. We also provide both theoretical analysis and empirical evidence about how this mechanism achieves adaptive suppression. This design transforms ``gradient vanishing'', traditionally a training bottleneck, into a principled noise-filtering shield for label-noise prompt tuning. Extensive experiments confirm that this simple, drop-in design achieves state-of-the-art robustness across various noisy benchmarks, outperforming methods with complex architectures and handcrafted hyperparameters.

中文摘要翻译: 像CLIP这样的对比视觉-语言模型展现出显著的零样本泛化能力。然而，提示调优对标签噪声仍然高度敏感，因为误标记样本会产生不成比例的大梯度，从而可能压倒预训练先验。我们认为，由于CLIP已经提供了接近最优的初始化，适应过程应该本质上是保守的，尤其是在噪声环境下面对极端梯度更新时。为此，我们提出了双Softmax提示调优（Double-Softmax Prompt Tuning, DSPT），一种无需超参数的内在梯度抑制方法。通过应用顺序概率归一化，DSPT诱导出一个自适应的饱和区域，该区域能够抑制高误差噪声样本的梯度，同时保留信息性更新。我们还提供了关于该机制如何实现自适应抑制的理论分析和实验证据。这一设计将传统上被视为训练瓶颈的“梯度消失”转化为一个原则性的噪声过滤屏障，用于含噪标签下的提示调优。大量实验证实，这种简单的即插即用设计在各种含噪基准测试中达到了最先进的鲁棒性，优于使用复杂架构和手工设计超参数的方法。

</details>


### [29] [Robust Fusion of Object-Level V2X for Learned 3D Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00595)
*Lukas Ostendorf,Lennart Reiher,Onn Haran,Lutz Eckstein*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究如何将V2X通信中的目标级信息集成到3D目标检测中，并针对现实V2X不完美性（噪声、目标丢失）提出噪声感知训练策略和显式置信度编码，提升系统鲁棒性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 车载传感器存在视线遮挡和视场角限制，导致遮挡或能见度差时感知失效。V2X通信可提供互补的目标级信息，但现实中的V2X存在延迟、定位误差、低渗透率等不完美性，需要研究如何鲁棒地融合这些信息。

Method: 基于nuScenes数据集，从真值仿真目标级协同感知消息，并注入可控噪声和目标丢失以模拟现实不完美性；将这些消息转换为专用BEV输入，融合到BEVFusion风格的检测器中；提出噪声感知训练策略和显式置信度编码以增强鲁棒性。

Result: 在理想条件下NDS达0.80，但基于理想数据训练的模型对V2X过度依赖、脆弱；所提噪声感知训练策略+显式置信度编码方法在严重噪声和低V2X渗透率下仍能保持性能增益。

Conclusion: 目标级协同信息能显著提升检测性能，但需通过噪声感知训练和置信度编码来增强对现实V2X不完美性的鲁棒性。

Original Abstract: Perception for automated driving is largely based on onboard environmental sensors, such as cameras and radar, which are cost-effective but limited by line-of-sight and field-of-view constraints. These inherent limitations may cause onboard perception to fail under occlusions or poor visibility conditions. In parallel, cooperative awareness via vehicle-to-everything (V2X) communication is becoming increasingly available, enabling vehicles and infrastructure to share their own state as object-level information that complements onboard perception. In this work, we study how such V2X information can be integrated into 3D object detection and how robust the resulting system is to realistic V2X imperfections. Using the nuScenes dataset, we emulate object-level cooperative awareness messages from ground truth, injecting controlled noise and object dropout to mimic real-world conditions such as latency, localization errors, and low V2X penetration rates. We convert these messages into a dedicated bird's-eye view (BEV) input and fuse them into a BEVFusion-style detector. Our results demonstrate that while object-level cooperative information can substantially improve detection performance, achieving an NDS of 0.80 under favorable conditions, models trained on idealized data become fragile and over-reliant on V2X. Conversely, our proposed noise-aware training strategy, coupled with explicit confidence encoding, enhances robustness, maintaining performance gains even under severe noise and reduced V2X penetration.

中文摘要翻译: 自动驾驶感知主要依赖于车载环境传感器，如摄像头和雷达，这些传感器成本低廉但受限于视线和视场角约束。这些固有局限性可能导致车载感知在遮挡或能见度差的条件下失效。与此同时，通过车联万物（V2X）通信实现的协同感知正变得越来越可用，使车辆和基础设施能够以目标级信息的形式共享自身状态，从而补充车载感知。在这项工作中，我们研究了如何将这类V2X信息集成到3D目标检测中，以及所得系统对现实V2X不完美性的鲁棒性如何。利用nuScenes数据集，我们从真值仿真目标级协同感知消息，注入受控噪声和目标丢失以模拟延迟、定位误差和低V2X渗透率等现实条件。我们将这些消息转换为专用的鸟瞰图（BEV）输入，并将其融合到BEVFusion风格的检测器中。我们的结果表明，虽然目标级协同信息可以显著提升检测性能（在有利条件下NDS达到0.80），但基于理想数据训练的模型变得脆弱且过度依赖V2X。相反，我们提出的噪声感知训练策略结合显式置信度编码增强了鲁棒性，即使在严重噪声和低V2X渗透率下也能保持性能增益。

</details>


### [30] [Faithful Extreme Image Rescaling with Learnable Reversible Transformation and Semantic Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00605)
*Hao Wei,Yanhui Zhou,Chenyang Ge,Saeed Anwar,Ajmal Mian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FaithEIR，一种基于扩散模型的极端图像缩放框架，利用可逆潜空间变换、高频字典先验和语义嵌入，在16倍以上缩放因子下实现高保真重建。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有极端图像缩放方法在高缩放因子（16×及以上）下难以保持语义一致的结构并生成逼真细节，因为低分辨率到高分辨率的映射是严重病态问题。

Method: 1) 受奇异值分解启发，提出可学习的可逆变换，实现潜空间中的可逆下采样和上采样；2) 提出自适应细节先验（高频字典），捕获训练数据中常见结构的经验平均值，补偿量化导致的信息损失；3) 设计轻量级像素语义嵌入器，为预训练扩散模型提供语义条件。

Result: 大量实验表明，FaithEIR在重建保真度和感知质量上 consistently 优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: FaithEIR通过可逆变换、高频字典先验和语义条件扩散模型，有效解决了极端图像缩放中的语义一致性和细节生成问题。

Original Abstract: Most recent extreme rescaling methods struggle to preserve semantically consistent structures and produce realistic details, due to the severely ill-posed nature of low- to high-resolution mapping under scaling factors of $16\times$ or higher. To alleviate the above problems, we propose FaithEIR, a diffusion-based framework for extreme image rescaling. Inspired by singular value decomposition, we develop learnable reversible transformation that enables invertible downscaling and upscaling in the latent space. To compensate for information loss due to quantization, we propose an adaptive detail prior, a high-frequency dictionary that captures the empirical average of commonly occurring structures in the training data. Finally, we design a lightweight pixel semantic embedder to provide semantic conditioning for the pretrained diffusion model. We present extensive experimental results demonstrating that our FaithEIR consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, achieving superior reconstruction fidelity and perceptual quality. Our code, model weights, and detailed results are released at https://github.com/cshw2021/FaithEIR.

中文摘要翻译: 大多数现有的极端图像缩放方法在16倍或更高缩放因子下，由于低分辨率到高分辨率映射的严重病态性，难以保持语义一致的结构并生成逼真的细节。为了缓解上述问题，我们提出了FaithEIR，一种基于扩散框架的极端图像缩放方法。受奇异值分解的启发，我们开发了可学习的可逆变换，能够在潜空间中实现可逆的下采样和上采样。为了补偿量化导致的信息损失，我们提出了一种自适应细节先验——一个高频字典，用于捕获训练数据中常见结构的经验平均值。最后，我们设计了一个轻量级的像素语义嵌入器，为预训练的扩散模型提供语义条件。我们展示了大量实验结果，证明FaithEIR consistently 优于最先进的方法，在重建保真度和感知质量方面均表现出色。我们的代码、模型权重和详细结果已发布在 https://github.com/cshw2021/FaithEIR。

</details>


### [31] [BlenderRAG: High-Fidelity 3D Object Generation via Retrieval-Augmented Code Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00632)
*Massimo Rondelli,Francesco Pivi,Maurizio Gabbrielli*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BlenderRAG是一个检索增强生成系统，通过多模态专家验证数据集和语义相似检索，在不需微调或专用硬件的情况下，将Blender代码的编译成功率从40.8%提升至70.0%，语义对齐从0.41提升至0.77。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前最先进的LLM从自然语言自动生成可执行的Blender代码时，频繁出现语法错误和几何不一致的对象，亟需一种无需微调且能有效提升生成质量的解决方案。

Method: 提出BlenderRAG，一个检索增强生成系统，构建包含500个专家验证的多模态示例（文本、代码、图像）的精选数据集，覆盖50个对象类别，在生成时通过检索语义相似的示例来增强LLM的输出。

Result: 在四种最先进的LLM上，BlenderRAG将编译成功率从40.8%提升至70.0%，语义归一化对齐（CLIP相似度）从0.41提升至0.77。

Conclusion: BlenderRAG无需微调或专用硬件即可显著提升LLM生成Blender代码的质量，具有即插即用的部署可行性。

Original Abstract: Automatic generation of executable Blender code from natural language remains challenging, with state-of-the-art LLMs producing frequent syntactic errors and geometrically inconsistent objects. We present BlenderRAG, a retrieval-augmented generation system that operates on a curated multimodal dataset of 500 expert-validated examples (text, code, image) across 50 object categories. By retrieving semantically similar examples during generation, BlenderRAG improves compilation success rates from 40.8% to 70.0% and semantic normalized alignment from 0.41 to 0.77 (CLIP similarity) across four state-of-the-art LLMs, without requiring fine-tuning or specialized hardware, making it immediately accessible for deployment. The dataset and code will be available at https://github.com/MaxRondelli/BlenderRAG.

中文摘要翻译: 从自然语言自动生成可执行的Blender代码仍然具有挑战性，最先进的LLM在生成过程中频繁出现语法错误和几何不一致的对象。我们提出BlenderRAG，一个检索增强生成系统，该系统在包含500个专家验证的示例（文本、代码、图像）的精选多模态数据集上运行，覆盖50个对象类别。通过在生成过程中检索语义相似的示例，BlenderRAG在四种最先进的LLM上将编译成功率从40.8%提升至70.0%，并将语义归一化对齐（CLIP相似度）从0.41提升至0.77，无需微调或专用硬件，使其立即可部署。数据集和代码将在https://github.com/MaxRondelli/BlenderRAG 上提供。

</details>


### [32] [InpaintSLat: Inpainting Structured 3D Latents via Initial Noise Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00664)
*Jaeyoung Chung,Suyoung Lee,Kyoung Mu Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需训练的3D修补方法，通过在结构化3D潜扩散框架中优化初始噪声，实现了高保真的上下文一致性与提示对齐。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在结构化3D潜扩散模型中，底层几何结构在扩散早期阶段建立，且对初始噪声高度敏感，这损害了修补和编辑任务的稳定性，因为模型需要在合成新结构的同时保证与现有上下文的严格对齐。

Method: 在结构化3D潜扩散框架中，利用基于整流流模型的反向传播近似来优化初始噪声，并采用频谱参数化实现鲁棒且高效的结构化3D潜空间优化。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在上下文一致性和提示对齐方面持续优于代表性的无需训练的修补基线，确立了初始噪声控制作为3D修补的一个独立维度。

Conclusion: 初始噪声控制可作为与传统的采样轨迹操控正交的独立维度，用于提升3D修补性能。

Original Abstract: We present a training-free approach for controllable 3D inpainting based on initial noise optimization. In the structured 3D latent diffusion framework, we observe that the underlying geometric structure is established during the early stages of the diffusion process and exhibits high sensitivity to the initial noise. Such characteristics compromise stability in tasks like inpainting and editing, where the model must ensure strict alignment with the existing context while synthesizing a new structure. In this paper, we introduce a strategy to optimize the initial noise within the structured 3D latent diffusion framework, ensuring high-fidelity 3D inpainting. Specifically, we update the initial noise by leveraging a backpropagation approximation grounded in the rectified flow model, with the spectral parameterization specially designed for robust and efficient structured 3D latent optimization. Experiments demonstrate consistent improvements in contextual consistency and prompt alignment over representative training-free inpainting baselines, establishing initial noise control as an independent dimension for 3D inpainting, orthogonal to conventional sampling trajectory manipulation.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了一种基于初始噪声优化的免训练可控3D修补方法。在结构化3D潜扩散框架中，我们观察到底层几何结构在扩散过程的早期阶段建立，并且对初始噪声高度敏感。这种特性在修补和编辑等任务中损害了稳定性，因为模型需要在合成新结构的同时保证与现有上下文的严格对齐。在本文中，我们引入了一种在结构化3D潜扩散框架内优化初始噪声的策略，确保了高保真的3D修补。具体来说，我们利用基于整流流模型的反向传播近似来更新初始噪声，并采用专门设计的频谱参数化以实现鲁棒且高效的结构化3D潜空间优化。实验表明，在上下文一致性和提示对齐方面，该方法持续优于代表性的免训练修补基线，确立了初始噪声控制作为3D修补的一个独立维度，与传统的采样轨迹操控正交。

</details>


### [33] [Prediction of Alzheimer's Disease Risk Factors from Retinal Images via Deep Learning: Development and Validation of Biologically Relevant Morphological Associations in the UK Biobank](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00665)
*Seowung Leem,Yunchao Yang,Adam J. Woods,Ruogu Fang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究利用深度学习模型从彩色眼底照片（CFP）中预测12种与阿尔茨海默病（AD）相关的风险因素，并探索眼底结构变化与AD易感性之间的关联。模型在部分任务上表现良好，显著性分析揭示视神经头和视网膜血管等生物相关区域，并在AD发病前平均8.55年的样本中发现了显著差异，表明CFP可能编码与AD风险相关的视网膜结构特征。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 系统性、代谢性和生活方式因素已通过流行病学和AD特异性生物标志物研究被证实与阿尔茨海默病相关，但彩色眼底照片（CFP）是否包含对应于这些AD风险因素的视网膜结构特征尚不清楚。本文旨在探究深度学习模型能否从CFP中预测AD相关风险因素，并表征这些预测背后的视网膜结构，从而评估CFP是否反映AD易感性的潜在通路。

Method: 利用UK Biobank的62,876张CFP图像（来自44,501名参与者），训练深度学习模型预测12种与AD发生率相关的因素（6个分类变量：性别、吸烟、失眠、经济状况、饮酒、抑郁；6个连续变量：年龄、受教育完成年龄、BMI、收缩压、舒张压、HbA1c）。评估模型性能、模型显著性图以及基于显著性得分的CAM-Score，并与视网膜形态学测量进行比较。同时，在AD发病前平均8.55年的病例与匹配对照组之间比较这些得分。

Result: 深度学习模型性能：分类变量AUROC范围为0.5654~0.9480，连续变量R²范围为-0.0291~0.7620，优于多数形态学-机器学习模型。基于显著性的得分一致性地突出了生物相关区域，尤其是视神经头和视网膜血管，并与现有的形态学变异一致。多个显著性得分在AD发病前案例与匹配对照组之间存在显著差异，提示风险因素的视网膜关联与临床前AD相关变化之间存在潜在重叠。

Conclusion: CFP编码了与AD风险因素相关的视网膜结构特征。尽管不具备诊断能力，但基于深度学习的视网膜表征可能揭示反映AD潜在易感性的生物相关风险结构变化。

Original Abstract: The systemic, metabolic, lifestyle factors have established associations with Alzheimer's Disease (AD) through epidemiologic and AD-specific biomarker studies. Whether colored fundus photography (CFP) contains retinal structural signatures corresponding to these AD-related risk domains remains unclear. To determine whether deep learning (DL) models can predict 12 AD-related risk factors from CFP and to characterize the retinal structures underlying these predictions, thereby assessing whether CFP reflects pathways to AD vulnerability. Using UK Biobank CFPs, DL models were trained using 62,876 images from 44,501 unique participants to predict 12 factors linked to AD incidence: 6 categorical (sex, smoking, sleeplessness, economic status, alcohol use, depression) and 6 continuous (age, age at completing education, BMI, systolic, diastolic blood pressure, HbA1c). Model performance, model saliency, and saliency-derived scores (CAM-Score) were evaluated and compared to retinal morphometry. The scores were also compared between incident-AD cases (average 8.55 years before onset) and matched controls. Performance of DL ranged from AUROC= 0.5654-0.9480 for categorical and R2=-0.0291-0.7620 for continuous factors, outperforming most of the morphometry-machine learning models. Saliency-based score consistently highlighted biologically meaningful regions, particularly the optic nerve head and retinal vasculature. It also aligned with present morphometric variations. Several saliency-based scores differed significantly between incident AD and matched controls, suggesting potential overlap between retinal correlates of risk factors and preclinical AD-associated changes. CFP encodes retinal signatures linked to AD risk factors. Although not diagnostic, DL-derived retinal representations may uncover biologically meaningful risk-related structural changes mirroring the potential AD vulnerability.

中文摘要翻译: 系统性、代谢性和生活方式因素已通过流行病学和AD特异性生物标志物研究被证实与阿尔茨海默病（AD）存在关联。然而，彩色眼底照片（CFP）是否包含对应于这些AD相关风险域的视网膜结构特征尚不清楚。本研究旨在探究深度学习（DL）模型能否从CFP中预测12种AD相关风险因素，并表征这些预测背后的视网膜结构，从而评估CFP是否反映AD易感性的潜在通路。利用UK Biobank的CFP图像，使用来自44,501名独特参与者的62,876张图像训练深度学习模型，以预测与AD发生率相关的12个因素：6个分类变量（性别、吸烟、失眠、经济状况、饮酒、抑郁）和6个连续变量（年龄、受教育完成年龄、BMI、收缩压、舒张压、HbA1c）。评估了模型性能、模型显著性图以及基于显著性得分的CAM-Score，并与视网膜形态学测量进行比较。这些得分还在AD发病前病例（平均发病前8.55年）与匹配对照组之间进行了比较。深度学习模型性能范围为：分类变量AUROC=0.5654~0.9480，连续变量R²=-0.0291~0.7620，优于大多数形态学-机器学习模型。基于显著性的得分一致性地突出了生物相关区域，特别是视神经头和视网膜血管，并与现有的形态学变异相一致。多个基于显著性的得分在AD发病前病例与匹配对照组之间存在显著差异，提示风险因素的视网膜关联与临床前AD相关变化之间存在潜在重叠。CFP编码了与AD风险因素相关的视网膜结构特征。尽管不具备诊断价值，但基于深度学习的视网膜表征可能揭示反映AD潜在易感性的生物相关风险结构变化。

</details>


### [34] [DMDSC: A Dynamic-Margin Deep Simplex Classifier for Open-Set Recognition on Medical Image Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00675)
*Vishal,Arnav Aditya,Nitin Kumar,Saurabh J. Shigwan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对医学影像数据集中的极端类别不平衡问题，本文提出DMDSC框架，通过动态边界方法自动调整各类别间距，对罕见病理实施更高惩罚和更紧密的特征聚类，在多个医学基准数据集上超越现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于神经坍缩的开放集识别方法（如DSC和UCDSC）采用统一边界，未考虑医学图像中不同类别的密度差异，无法有效应对数据不平衡带来的挑战。

Method: 提出DMDSC框架，引入动态边界方法：基于标签频率自动调整类别特定的边界，对稀有病理类别施加更高惩罚和更紧密的特征聚类，以抵消数据不平衡的影响。

Result: 在BloodMNIST、OCTMNIST、DermaMNIST和BreaKHis等多个医学基准数据集上的广泛实验表明，所提框架优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: 提出的DMDSC通过动态边界机制有效解决了医学图像开放集识别中的类别不平衡问题，显著提升了模型在稀有病理类别上的识别能力。

Original Abstract: Medical imaging datasets are often characterized by extreme class imbalances, where rare pathologies are significantly underrepresented compared to common conditions. This imbalance poses a dual challenge for Open-Set Recognition (OSR): models must maintain high classification accuracy on known classes while reliably rejecting unknown samples unseen during training in the clinical settings. While recently proposed Deep Simplex Classifier (DSC)~\cite{cevikalp2024reaching} and UnCertainty-aware Deep Simplex Classifier (UCDSC)~\cite{Aditya_2026_WACV} successfully leverage Neural Collapse to ensure maximal inter-class separation, they rely on a uniform margin that does not account for the varying densities of medical classes.
  In this paper, we propose DMDSC an enhanced framework featuring a dynamic margin approach. Our approach automatically adapts class-specific margins based on label frequency, enforcing a higher penalty and tighter feature clustering for rare pathologies to counteract the effects of data imbalance. Extensive experiments conducted on diverse medical benchmarks on BloodMNIST\cite{medmnistv2}, OCTMNIST\cite{medmnistv2}, DermaMNIST\cite{medmnistv2}, and BreaKHis~\cite{spanhol2015dataset} datasets, demonstrate that our framework outperforms state-of-the-art methods.

中文摘要翻译: 医学影像数据集通常具有极端的类别不平衡特征，其中罕见病理相较于常见病变的样本量显著不足。这种不平衡给开放集识别带来了双重挑战：模型必须在保持已知类别高分类精度的同时，在临床场景下可靠地拒绝训练中未出现的未知样本。尽管近期提出的深度单纯形分类器和不确定性感知深度单纯形分类器成功利用神经坍缩确保了最大化的类间分离，但它们依赖于统一的边界，未能考虑医学类别中不同密度的差异。本文提出DMDSC，一个增强型框架，采用动态边界方法。我们的方法基于标签频率自动调整类别特定的边界，对罕见病理施加更高惩罚和更紧密的特征聚类，以抵消数据不平衡的影响。在BloodMNIST、OCTMNIST、DermaMNIST和BreaKHis等多个医学基准数据集上进行的大量实验表明，我们的框架优于现有最先进方法。

### [35] [Foundation AI Models for Aerosol Optical Depth Estimation from PACE Satellite Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00678)
*Zahid Hassan Tushar,Sanjay Purushotham*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出 ViTCG 模型，利用 Vision Transformer 和通道分组空间回归从高光谱图像中反演气溶胶光学厚度，相比现有基础模型均方误差降低 62%，并能生成空间一致的结果。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于物理的 AOD 反演方法依赖辐射传输模型、查表法和辅助气象数据，计算量大且空间一致性差；数据驱动方法未充分利用高光谱图像的空间-光谱相干性，导致反演结果存在空间不一致和对噪声敏感的问题。

Method: 提出 ViTCG（Vision Transformer with Channel-wise Grouping），以高光谱大气顶部辐射亮度为输入，通过通道分组策略和空间回归框架联合建模空间上下文与光谱信息，实现端到端的 AOD 反演。

Result: 基于 PACE 辐射观测数据的验证表明，ViTCG 相比 Prithvi 等最先进基础模型，均方误差降低 62%，并能生成空间连贯的 AOD 场。

Conclusion: 首次将基础 AI 模型用于 AOD 反演，ViTCG 通过联合建模空间-光谱信息显著提升了反演精度和空间一致性。

Original Abstract: Aerosol Optical Depth (AOD) retrieval is essential for Earth observation, supporting applications from air quality monitoring to climate studies. We present the first study exploring Foundation AI models for AOD retrieval and propose ViTCG, a Vision Transformer with Channel-wise Grouping-based spatial regression framework that reduces retrieval bias and error. ViTCG uses hyperspectral top-of-atmosphere radiance as input and jointly models spatial context and spectral information. Validation with PACE radiance observations demonstrates a 62% reduction in mean squared error compared to state-of-the-art foundation models, including Prithvi, and produces spatially coherent AOD fields.

中文摘要翻译: 气溶胶光学厚度（AOD）反演对于地球观测至关重要，支撑着从空气质量监测到气候研究的诸多应用。传统的基于物理的 AOD 反演方法将问题建模为逐像素反演，依赖辐射传输建模、内存密集型的查找表以及辅助气象数据。尽管近年来的数据驱动方法展现出潜力，但许多方法未能利用高光谱影像的空间-光谱相干性，导致反演结果空间不一致且对噪声敏感。本文首次探索基础 AI 模型用于 AOD 反演，并提出 ViTCG——一种结合通道分组空间回归框架的视觉 Transformer，可减少反演偏差与误差。ViTCG 以高光谱大气顶部辐射亮度为输入，联合建模空间上下文与光谱信息。基于 PACE 辐射观测数据的验证表明，与包括 Prithvi 在内的最先进基础模型相比，ViTCG 的均方误差降低了 62%，并能生成空间连贯的 AOD 场。
